# Conscious Activations Atomic Harness Pipeline — Source-First Interview Production, Brownfield Runtime Activation, and Programmed Models PRD

**Version:** 1.1.0-draft  
**Status:** DRAFT FOR HUMAN RATIFICATION  
**Prepared:** 2026-07-21

# Document Purpose and Authority

This PRD amends and deepens `CA-AHP-PRD-V1`. It defines the Atomic Harness Pipeline as the governed execution product that consumes Builder-produced Atomic Harnesses and coordinates source-backed content production. The primary correction is that interview-derived production begins from one canonical source package, not from disconnected format requests.

The talking-head interview video, transcript, speakers, word and phrase timestamps, tags, audio events, Expression Moments, keyframes, rights, and provenance form the canonical source package. Brief-led Activative Interviews and imported interview videos are equal first-class admission paths after validation. For source-led short videos, the original talking-head footage remains the A-roll spine. Carousels, SuperVisuals, and authorized animation derivatives preserve exact source and transformation lineage even when the original footage is not visible.

This document preserves current Builder, VAE, Delegation, Interview Expression, Studio, and Program Control product boundaries. It uses the CMF Studio predecessor as brownfield implementation and test evidence, not as current semantic authority. It also enforces the Studio V2.1 correction: the Atomic Harness conducts production; the Studio supervises, corrects, and ships; every meaningful human resolution becomes scoped programming material; Format 02 remains deferred.

## Authority order

1. Activative Intelligence and Visual Narrative Constitution V1.1.
2. Current Program Control authority and reconciled product status.
3. Current approved Builder, Interview Expression, VAE, Delegation, and Studio product authorities and contracts.
4. Ratified decisions D001–D054.
5. This PRD after explicit human ratification.
6. Current implementation and accepted predecessor evidence according to exact source dispositions.
7. External-project research evidence after license, security, and architecture review.

## Status caution

The supplied reconciliation file states that public repository status is older than operator-reported local terminal campaigns. Implementation remains blocked until exact bytes and receipts are verified and Program Control publishes one current status. This PRD grants no implementation, cloud, model-training, participant, publication, production, or certification authority.


# Vision and Product Promise

## Vision

Conscious Activations should operate as one source-expression production system. A real human interview becomes a trusted, richly indexed source package. Atomic Harnesses then compile different category-native embodiments of that source: source-led short videos, Carousels, SuperVisuals, and separately authorized animation derivatives. The system should automate editing and composition with the precision of a specialized production team while preserving human truth, Activative purpose, source lineage, product sovereignty, and human creative authority.

## Product promise

> Given an accepted Canonical Interview Source Package or Asset Package Spec, current Atomic Harnesses, authorized execution bindings, and a campaign order, the Atomic Harness Pipeline compiles a source-backed content batch; retrieves the exact Skills, Steering Recipes, precedents, tools, and models needed by each Workflow Node; preserves talking-head A-roll for source-led shorts; realizes static, temporal, and delegated visual programs through approved embodiments; independently evaluates and selectively repairs outputs; exposes category-native supervision; records every human resolution as scoped programming material; and emits real, replayable source-to-artifact evidence without changing the source or Harness meaning.

## Core operating flow

Activative Interview Brief-led session or imported interview  
→ Canonical Interview Source Package  
→ tag, phrase, shot, keyframe, and Expression Moment governance  
→ Expression Ingredient Inventory / Asset Package Spec  
→ content-batch and archetype routing  
→ Builder-produced Atomic Harnesses and execution bindings  
→ authority-first retrieval and JIT Capsules  
→ Workflow Nodes and bounded roles  
→ VideoEditProgram / Composition IR / animation program / Visual Asset Demand  
→ FFmpeg / Remotion / HyperFrames / Skia / VAE and eligible workers  
→ deterministic and independent evaluation  
→ selective repair or human resolution  
→ source-grounded artifacts, publication evidence, and learning episodes


# Users, Jobs, and Journeys

## Primary users

- Conscious Content Operator and creative-policy authority.
- Interview Expression operator and expression-evidence reviewer.
- Harness Architect and Builder operator.
- Pipeline operator and reliability engineer.
- Static, video, animation, VAE, and runtime adapter engineer.
- Retrieval, Programmed Model, and evaluator engineer.
- Human approver with a recorded bounded authority scope.
- Program Control release and evidence authority.

## Core jobs

- Admit either an Activative Interview session or existing interview media without losing or fabricating history.
- Convert one trusted interview source into a coordinated batch of category-native derivative jobs.
- Preserve source truth, quotes, evidence, voice, identity, and exact time/frame lineage.
- Produce source-led talking-head shorts without manually reconstructing every cut.
- Produce Carousels, SuperVisuals, and authorized animation derivatives from the same expression material.
- Retrieve only eligible Skills, Steering Recipes, examples, tools, and model claims for the current node.
- Supervise campaigns, resolve genuine taste or authority decisions, and request exact corrections.
- Turn corrections into scoped programming material without uncontrolled live self-modification.
- Operate, cancel, replay, restore, audit, ship, and expand the system truthfully.

### UJ-01 — Admit an Activative Interview session

The operator uses an approved Activative Interview Brief and recording to create a source package that distinguishes planned activation from actual human expression.

### UJ-02 — Admit an imported interview

The operator uploads existing talking-head footage and transcript and receives the same trusted production entry point without fabricated Brief history.

### UJ-03 — Inspect and approve source expression

Hunters propose tags and Expression Moments; Analysts inspect source context; authorized reviewers approve, reject, or restrict material.

### UJ-04 — Launch one source-backed content batch

The operator selects outputs, Harnesses, budget, deadline, and autonomy mode; the Pipeline compiles derivative jobs from one source package.

### UJ-05 — Produce a talking-head short

The original interview footage remains A-roll while the system selects word-safe spans, adds source-supporting visuals, renders, evaluates, and repairs.

### UJ-06 — Produce a Carousel

Approved quotes, evidence, Expression Moments, and keyframes become a slide-native, source-grounded sequence.

### UJ-07 — Produce a SuperVisual

One approved premise or proof becomes a feed-legible single-frame argument with exact lineage.

### UJ-08 — Produce a 2D animation derivative

A separately authorized animation Harness uses source audio, quotes, evidence, keyframes, and identity references without activating Format 02.

### UJ-09 — Acquire a missing visual ingredient

A source-backed demand crosses Delegation to VAE, which may use registered capabilities such as SAM3, Lucida, ComfyUI, layered providers, or bounded GNM geometry.

### UJ-10 — Evaluate and repair a local failure

Rendered output is mechanically checked, independently evaluated, diagnosed, and selectively rerun.

### UJ-11 — Correct production in natural language or by direct manipulation

The Studio compiles the operator's request or UI delta into a typed ChangeRequestProgram and records the result as a HumanResolutionEpisode.

### UJ-12 — Run in the appropriate autonomy mode

A mature Harness operates in Autopilot or Review Before Ship, while Checkpointed and Shadow modes enforce declared gates and publication limits.

### UJ-13 — Retrieve the right Skill, recipe, tool, and precedent

Deterministic filters and hybrid retrieval compile Minimum Complete Context for the current node.

### UJ-14 — Promote a Programmed Model claim

A model team builds rights-aware data, proves held-out advantage, shadows the claim, and obtains bounded human promotion.

### UJ-15 — Contain a regression

The system quarantines the affected claim or runtime, routes to a known-good fallback, and restores only after evidence.

### UJ-16 — Ship and audit the batch

The operator accepts or publishes eligible outputs and exports complete source-to-artifact evidence and replay packages.


# Canonical Glossary

| Term | Canonical meaning |
|---|---|
| Canonical Interview Source Package | Immutable root object binding source video/audio, transcript, speakers, timestamps, tags, shots, keyframes, Expression Moments, rights, and provenance. |
| Activative Interview Brief | Pre-session design describing intended Context Premises, Matrix of Edging, anchors, asset opportunities, and activation conditions; it is not proof of actual expression. |
| Imported Interview Admission | First-class admission of existing interview media and transcript without claiming a historical Activative Brief existed. |
| Tag Provenance State | Planned, observed, inferred, operator-confirmed, rejected, or superseded state for a source or routing tag. |
| Packed Phrase Transcript | Compact, deterministic, speaker- and time-aware reasoning view derived from canonical word-level transcription. |
| Anchor Hit | Source-backed candidate moment that may support deeper expression discovery but is not automatically an approved Expression Moment. |
| Expression Moment | Approved source span with exact words/time, context, speaker, expression qualities, evidence, restrictions, and derivative potential. |
| Expression Ingredient Inventory | Approved source-backed quotes, evidence, moments, keyframes, voice/audio references, tags, restrictions, and route opportunities. |
| Asset Package Spec | Interview Expression handoff that packages the Expression Ingredient Inventory for downstream Atomic Harnesses. |
| Content Batch Orchestration Program | Pipeline-owned graph of derivative jobs, Harnesses, shared source analysis, dependencies, budgets, review policies, and lineage. |
| Content Derivative Job | Immutable request binding one source grant, Harness, category/profile, output, evaluation, rights, runtime needs, and review policy. |
| AtomicHarnessDefinition | Builder-owned immutable semantic and operational constitution for one Atomic Harness. |
| HarnessExecutionBindingManifest | Immutable deployment mapping from Harness requirements to exact implementations, humans, products, Programmed Models, and runtime embodiments. |
| Workflow Node | Smallest executable operation in a Pipeline graph. |
| Hunter / Analyst / Composer / Commander | Explicit workflow roles for candidate discovery, evidence verification, program compilation, and transition authorization; not hidden personas. |
| Canonical Skill | Stable reusable procedure and invariants. |
| Steering Recipe | Evidence-backed conditional visual or editing strategy with applicability, intervention, protected properties, failures, lifecycle, and rollback. |
| Transformation Contract | Must-remain-true conditions, required changes, creative degrees of freedom, and wrong-reading locks for one transformation. |
| Composition IR | Renderer-neutral static visual program. |
| VideoEditProgram | Canonical adopted temporal editing program based on predecessor edit/timeline contracts and extended for current source lineage and runtime/evaluation bindings. |
| A-roll Spine | Original talking-head source footage and audio forming the base timeline of a source-led short. |
| Temporal Embodiment | Approved runtime such as Remotion, HyperFrames, FFmpeg, or a bounded animation runtime that realizes an accepted program. |
| Programmed Model | Versioned post-trained model artifact plus a bounded learned capability claim. |
| Model Program | Governed deployment of a Programmed Model with JIT context, tools, validators, evaluator, budget, fallback, and receipts. |
| HumanResolutionEpisode | Immutable record of a meaningful human decision, exact before/after state, operations, evidence, authority, result, and scoped learning dispositions. |
| ChangeRequestProgram | Typed minimal tool program compiled from operator language or direct manipulation. |
| StudioSurfaceBinding | Harness-to-Studio routing record declaring primary/supporting modules, visible evidence, permitted commands, and entry policy. |
| GNM | Google Generative aNthropometric Model; VAE-owned bounded facial-geometry capability, never human identity or emotional truth authority. |
| Format 02 Activation Gate | Requirement that the current Builder emit and independent validation accept the complete current Format 02 Harness before any active runtime or Studio path exists. |

# Doctrine and Product Principles

1. **Activation First remains the runtime law.** The Pipeline executes upstream Activative and source authority; it does not invent it.
2. **Visual Syntax First remains a Harness-development discovery law and cannot be reinterpreted by runtime adapters.**
3. **The canonical interview source package is the root of interview-derived production.**
4. **Activative Interview Brief intent and actual human expression remain separate.**
5. **Talking-head A-roll remains the base timeline for source-led shorts.**
6. **All derivative formats preserve exact source, quote/evidence, keyframe, voice, and transformation lineage.**
7. **Builder remains canonical; Pipeline never creates a second Harness truth.**
8. **Workflow Nodes and explicit roles replace monolithic hidden agents.**
9. **Retrieval eligibility precedes semantic or visual ranking.**
10. **Stable competence may live in Programmed Model weights; current truth, rights, doctrine, and evidence remain explicit context.**
11. **Skills define stable behavior; Steering Recipes define evidence-backed conditional strategy; runtime bindings define embodiment.**
12. **Renderers and providers realize accepted programs and cannot acquire creative or semantic authority.**
13. **Human decisions become programming material automatically, but live weights and doctrine do not mutate automatically.**
14. **Studio is a supervisory, correction, evidence, and shipping surface; canonical state remains in product services.**
15. **VAE owns visual production methods, including GNM; GNM geometry does not define a real person's identity or emotion.**
16. **Format 02 remains deferred until its current Harness activation gate passes.**
17. **Mechanical facts are proven mechanically; judgment is independently evaluated; unresolved meaning, consent, identity, policy, and taste route to humans.**
18. **Real files, hashes, process receipts, and replay evidence outrank synthetic references or self-reported success.**

# F01 — Product Authority, Brownfield Baseline, and Source Reconciliation

## 1. Product claim and user outcome

**User outcome:** The product begins from current constitutional authority, verified product status, and the tested CMF Studio predecessor instead of a greenfield rewrite.

Establish one trustworthy implementation baseline, preserve exact provenance, and prevent predecessor code or stale status from silently becoming current authority. This feature exists to convert doctrine and source evidence into behavior that can be implemented, tested, denied, replayed, and audited. It does not grant implementation, provider, model-training, publication, production, or certification authority by itself.

## 2. Product boundary and ownership

The owning product is the Atomic Harness Pipeline unless an FR explicitly assigns Interview Expression, VAE, Delegation, Studio, Program Control, or an external runtime.

The feature must preserve the current product topology. Builder supplies the immutable Atomic Harness; Pipeline executes its declared nodes; Interview Expression owns source expression preparation and approval; VAE owns visual production; Delegation owns cross-product envelopes; Studio projects state and emits typed operator commands; Program Control owns cross-product authority and release truth. External renderers and models are embodiments, not sources of meaning.

## 3. Canonical objects and state

The feature consumes current, versioned upstream records and emits typed outputs that remain linked to the active Harness, source package where applicable, Workflow Node, JIT Capsule, execution binding, evaluator, and receipt. Canonical records use stable serialization and immutable identities. A UI projection, model response, provider job, renderer workspace, or local cache cannot become accepted product state until its contract and authority gates pass.

Core invariants for this feature are:

- Current Program Control precedence is checked before action.
- Brownfield source use carries exact disposition and provenance.
- Implementation and evidence claims remain separate.

## 4. Brownfield and external capability treatment

The implementation begins from exact current and predecessor evidence. The table below identifies the most relevant source records. `REUSE` or `ADAPT` permits bounded implementation reuse after namespace, authority, license, dependency, and behavior review; it never imports historical product meaning automatically.

| Source | Disposition | Exact path or reference | Role |
|---|---|---|---|
| `SRC-CUR-001` | `REFERENCE` | CMF_PROGRAM_CONTROL/00_CONSTITUTION/CONSTITUTIONAL_AUTHORITY.md | Constitutional precedence and current product-authority pointer. |
| `SRC-CUR-002` | `REFERENCE` | CMF_PROGRAM_CONTROL/00_CONSTITUTION/current-v1.1/docs/00_ACTIVATIVE_SYSTEM_CONSTITUTION.md | Activation First, Visual Syntax First, product topology and semantic lineage. |
| `SRC-CUR-003` | `REFERENCE` | CMF_PROGRAM_CONTROL/03_PROGRAM_STATUS/MASTER_STATUS.md | Public repository convergence and authorization status observed 2026-07-15. |
| `SRC-CUR-011` | `REFERENCE` | 01_ATOMIC_HARNESS_BUILDER/CURRENT_PROJECT_STATUS.md | Public Builder status snapshot; must be reconciled with newer operator-local receipts before implementation. |
| `SRC-LEG-033` | `RETAIN_EVIDENCE` | docs/audits/CMF_VISUAL_GEOMETRICS_SKIA_SAM3_PRETEXT_AUDIT_2026-06-24.md | Existing execution-spine audit. |
| `SRC-LEG-034` | `RETAIN_EVIDENCE` | docs/prd/modules/PRD_CMF_07_Editing_Composition_Rendering.md | Legacy editing/composition/rendering intent. |

## 5. Workflow integration

Validated upstream state → feature behavior → typed output and receipt → downstream handoff → evaluation, invalidation, and replay.

Every handoff is typed. A downstream node begins only after the producer output passes the declared contract and evidence gates. Failures are attributed to source, knowledge, retrieval, Skill, recipe, Programmed Model, tool, runtime, product, evaluator, or human-policy layers before repair or escalation.

## 6. Functional Requirements

### FR-001 — Use current authority precedence

**Lifecycle:** `PRESERVED_AND_DEEPENED`  
**Normative requirement:** The Pipeline shall read Program Control authority and the current Builder/VAE/Delegation product boundaries before accepting any executable binding.

**Trigger and preconditions:** When a validated run, planning action, or operator request requires `Use current authority precedence` within feature F01.

**Required output or state transition:** A versioned, inspectable result or governed record that satisfies this requirement and can be consumed by the declared downstream owner.

**Authority and invariants:**
- Current Program Control precedence is checked before action.
- Brownfield source use carries exact disposition and provenance.
- Implementation and evidence claims remain separate.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given current authority, valid inputs, and an eligible execution binding, when this behavior runs, then the Pipeline shall read Program Control authority and the current Builder/VAE/Delegation product boundaries before accepting any executable binding and the downstream consumer receives a contract-valid result.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given stale, ineligible, ambiguous, out-of-scope, or unverifiable inputs, when this behavior is requested, then no unauthorized side effect occurs and a typed blocker names the cause, owner, and next admissible action.
- **Evidence required:** authority/status reconciliation, source disposition, provenance hashes, license review, and denial tests, linked to an immutable requirement receipt.

**Governing decisions:** D001, D002, D003, D004, D027  
**Exact source references:** SRC-CUR-001, SRC-CUR-002, SRC-CUR-003, SRC-CUR-011, SRC-LEG-033, SRC-LEG-034

- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given stale, ineligible, ambiguous, out-of-scope, or unverifiable inputs, when this behavior is requested, then no unauthorized side effect occurs and a typed blocker names the cause, owner, and next admissible action.

### FR-006 — Require replacement justification

**Lifecycle:** `PRESERVED_AND_DEEPENED`  
**Normative requirement:** A greenfield replacement of a working predecessor component requires an explicit gap, contract mismatch or bounded-cost justification.

**Trigger and preconditions:** When a validated run, planning action, or operator request requires `Require replacement justification` within feature F01.

**Required output or state transition:** A versioned, inspectable result or governed record that satisfies this requirement and can be consumed by the declared downstream owner.

**Authority and invariants:**
- Current Program Control precedence is checked before action.
- Brownfield source use carries exact disposition and provenance.
- Implementation and evidence claims remain separate.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given current authority, valid inputs, and an eligible execution binding, when this behavior runs, then a greenfield replacement of a working predecessor component requires an explicit gap, contract mismatch or bounded-cost justification and the downstream consumer receives a contract-valid result.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given stale, ineligible, ambiguous, out-of-scope, or unverifiable inputs, when this behavior is requested, then no unauthorized side effect occurs and a typed blocker names the cause, owner, and next admissible action.
- **Evidence required:** authority/status reconciliation, source disposition, provenance hashes, license review, and denial tests, linked to an immutable requirement receipt.

**Governing decisions:** D001, D002, D003, D004, D027  
**Exact source references:** SRC-CUR-001, SRC-CUR-002, SRC-CUR-003, SRC-CUR-011, SRC-LEG-033, SRC-LEG-034


## 7. Execution, model, tool, and human responsibilities

Deterministic services own mechanically decidable facts. Programmed Models or bounded Agent Programs may propose or compile behavior only within their evidence-backed claim and node-local tool grants. Independent evaluators inspect judgment dimensions. Humans own new meaning, consent, identity, unresolved taste, policy exceptions, promotion, and publication authority where assigned. The producing model or runtime cannot accept its own output.

When the feature uses a Hunter, Analyst, Composer, or Commander role, the role is an explicit workflow responsibility. It may be implemented by code, a small model, a larger model, or a human. The role name never hides the actual actor or expand its authority.

## 8. Validation and quality gates

Validation must prove both the intended result and the process that produced it. The minimum feature evidence includes authority/status reconciliation, source disposition, provenance hashes, license review, and denial tests. Mechanical tests run before expensive model or visual evaluation. Judgment evaluators are calibrated to the exact category and context. Every denial names the cause, owner, and next admissible action. Every accepted mutation emits an immutable receipt and updates only dependent state.

## 9. Risks, mitigations, and stop conditions

| Risk | Concrete consequence | Mitigation |
|---|---|---|
| Authority drift | A predecessor, external project, UI, model, or renderer is treated as current product authority. | Require exact source disposition, current authority validation, and product-boundary tests. |
| False completion | A synthetic URI, dry-run, unverified command, or model self-report is promoted as a real result. | Require actual files, hashes, independent validation, and artifact-class labels. |
| Over-broad automation | A model or agent gains tools, context, or authority beyond the current node. | Use JIT context, node-local tool grants, sandboxes, and explicit escalation. |
| Hidden mutation | Accepted meaning, source, program, or human preference changes without a versioned record. | Use immutable versions, typed commands, receipts, and selective invalidation. |

**Stop conditions**

- The behavior would create a second semantic or canonical state owner.
- A required source, right, authority, contract, runtime, evaluator, or human decision is unavailable or unverified.
- The implementation would treat migration evidence or an external project as current authority.
- The change would imply real output, production readiness, or certification beyond available evidence.

## 10. Planning and implementation handoff

This module is implementation-ready only after its FRs have one primary vertical Story owner, its Stories pass CBAR hardening, its candidate Tech Specs identify exact existing code and target paths, and Program Control issues a bounded Development Capsule. Until then, this module is a product-authority draft.

*This feature module belongs to the Conscious Activations Atomic Harness Pipeline PRD V1.1 source-first reconciliation package.*


---

# F02 — Atomic Harness Intake and Execution Binding

## 1. Product claim and user outcome

**User outcome:** The Pipeline consumes the existing AtomicHarnessDefinition and binds it to approved implementations without creating a second Harness truth.

Turn an immutable Builder product into an executable deployment binding while keeping meaning and implementation separate. This feature exists to convert doctrine and source evidence into behavior that can be implemented, tested, denied, replayed, and audited. It does not grant implementation, provider, model-training, publication, production, or certification authority by itself.

## 2. Product boundary and ownership

The owning product is the Atomic Harness Pipeline unless an FR explicitly assigns Interview Expression, VAE, Delegation, Studio, Program Control, or an external runtime.

The feature must preserve the current product topology. Builder supplies the immutable Atomic Harness; Pipeline executes its declared nodes; Interview Expression owns source expression preparation and approval; VAE owns visual production; Delegation owns cross-product envelopes; Studio projects state and emits typed operator commands; Program Control owns cross-product authority and release truth. External renderers and models are embodiments, not sources of meaning.

## 3. Canonical objects and state

The feature consumes current, versioned upstream records and emits typed outputs that remain linked to the active Harness, source package where applicable, Workflow Node, JIT Capsule, execution binding, evaluator, and receipt. Canonical records use stable serialization and immutable identities. A UI projection, model response, provider job, renderer workspace, or local cache cannot become accepted product state until its contract and authority gates pass.

Core invariants for this feature are:

- Builder remains canonical.
- Bindings select implementations but do not mutate Harness semantics.
- Unresolved capability ownership blocks side effects.

## 4. Brownfield and external capability treatment

The implementation begins from exact current and predecessor evidence. The table below identifies the most relevant source records. `REUSE` or `ADAPT` permits bounded implementation reuse after namespace, authority, license, dependency, and behavior review; it never imports historical product meaning automatically.

| Source | Disposition | Exact path or reference | Role |
|---|---|---|---|
| `SRC-CUR-004` | `REFERENCE` | 01_ATOMIC_HARNESS_BUILDER/src/cmf_builder/domain/atomic_harness_definition.py | Canonical AtomicHarnessDefinition structure and execution-free status. |
| `SRC-CUR-008` | `REFERENCE` | 01_ATOMIC_HARNESS_BUILDER/src/cmf_builder/domain/capability_ownership.py | Current broad Capability Ownership graph and explicit handoff evidence. |
| `SRC-CUR-010` | `REFERENCE` | 01_ATOMIC_HARNESS_BUILDER/src/cmf_builder/workflow/actor_explicit_contracts.py | Execution-free Workflow Node, edge, authority and validation contracts. |
| `SRC-LEG-001` | `ADAPT` | src/ccp_studio/contracts/studio_pipeline_recipe_harness.py | Old recipe/step contracts become a compatibility input to Workflow IR; they cannot define current meaning. |

## 5. Workflow integration

Validated upstream state → feature behavior → typed output and receipt → downstream handoff → evaluation, invalidation, and replay.

Every handoff is typed. A downstream node begins only after the producer output passes the declared contract and evidence gates. Failures are attributed to source, knowledge, retrieval, Skill, recipe, Programmed Model, tool, runtime, product, evaluator, or human-policy layers before repair or escalation.

## 6. Functional Requirements

**Trigger and preconditions:** When a validated run, planning action, or operator request requires `Load exact AtomicHarnessDefinition` within feature F02.

**Required output or state transition:** A versioned, inspectable result or governed record that satisfies this requirement and can be consumed by the declared downstream owner.

**Authority and invariants:**
- Builder remains canonical.
- Bindings select implementations but do not mutate Harness semantics.
- Unresolved capability ownership blocks side effects.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given current authority, valid inputs, and an eligible execution binding, when this behavior runs, then the Pipeline shall ingest a portable AtomicHarnessDefinition package and verify schema, identity, hash, authority, lineage, category/profile and invalidation state and the downstream consumer receives a contract-valid result.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given stale, ineligible, ambiguous, out-of-scope, or unverifiable inputs, when this behavior is requested, then no unauthorized side effect occurs and a typed blocker names the cause, owner, and next admissible action.
- **Evidence required:** schema/hash validation, graph reconciliation, binding manifest, compatibility tests, supersession and replay, linked to an immutable requirement receipt.

# F03 — Workflow Node Execution Kernel and Bounded Role Taxonomy

## 1. Product claim and user outcome

**User outcome:** The Pipeline executes explicit Workflow Nodes within governed Phase boundaries and keeps actor, ownership, role, authority, and product boundary distinct.

Provide the smallest auditable unit of execution and represent Hunters, Analysts, Composers, Commanders, humans, deterministic modules, models, and products without hidden ownership. This feature exists to convert doctrine and source evidence into behavior that can be implemented, tested, denied, replayed, and audited. It does not grant implementation, provider, model-training, publication, production, or certification authority by itself.

## 2. Product boundary and ownership

The owning product is the Atomic Harness Pipeline unless an FR explicitly assigns Interview Expression, VAE, Delegation, Studio, Program Control, or an external runtime.

The feature must preserve the current product topology. External renderers and models are embodiments, not sources of meaning.

## 3. Canonical objects and state

The feature consumes current, versioned upstream records and emits typed outputs that remain linked to the active Harness, source package where applicable, Workflow Node, JIT Capsule, execution binding, evaluator, and receipt. A UI projection, model response, provider job, renderer workspace, or local cache cannot become accepted product state until its contract and authority gates pass.

Core invariants for this feature are:

- Every node has one declared actor and owner.
- Handoffs are typed and validated.
- Roles never imply authority beyond their assigned node.

- **Primary success:** Given current authority, valid inputs, and an eligible execution binding, when this behavior runs, then every node attempt shall record inputs, JIT Capsule, implementation, actions, output, validation, status, timing, cost and lineage and the downstream consumer receives a contract-valid result.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given stale, ineligible, ambiguous, out-of-scope, or unverifiable inputs, when this behavior is requested, then no unauthorized side effect occurs and a typed blocker names the cause, owner, and next admissible action.
- **Evidence required:** graph validation, scheduling tests, handoff conformance, actor/role matrices, and node receipts, linked to an immutable requirement receipt.

**Governing decisions:** D009, D010, D011, D020, D037  
**Exact source references:** SRC-CUR-007, SRC-CUR-008, SRC-CUR-010, SRC-LEG-001, SRC-LEG-002, SRC-LEG-003


## 7. Execution, model, tool, and human responsibilities

Deterministic services own mechanically decidable facts. Programmed Models or bounded Agent Programs may propose or compile behavior only within their evidence-backed claim and node-local tool grants. Independent evaluators inspect judgment dimensions. Humans own new meaning, consent, identity, unresolved taste, policy exceptions, promotion, and publication authority where assigned. The producing model or runtime cannot accept its own output.

When the feature uses a Hunter, Analyst, Composer, or Commander role, the role is an explicit workflow responsibility. It may be implemented by code, a small model, a larger model, or a human. The role name never hides the actual actor or expand its authority.

## 8. Validation and quality gates

Validation must prove both the intended result and the process that produced it. The minimum feature evidence includes graph validation, scheduling tests, handoff conformance, actor/role matrices, and node receipts. Mechanical tests run before expensive model or visual evaluation. Judgment evaluators are calibrated to the exact category and context. Every denial names the cause, owner, and next admissible action. Every accepted mutation emits an immutable receipt and updates only dependent state.

## 9. Risks, mitigations, and stop conditions

| Risk | Concrete consequence | Mitigation |
|---|---|---|
| Authority drift | A predecessor, external project, UI, model, or renderer is treated as current product authority. | Require exact source disposition, current authority validation, and product-boundary tests. |
| False completion | A synthetic URI, dry-run, unverified command, or model self-report is promoted as a real result. | Require actual files, hashes, independent validation, and artifact-class labels. |
| Over-broad automation | A model or agent gains tools, context, or authority beyond the current node. | Use JIT context, node-local tool grants, sandboxes, and explicit escalation. |
| Hidden mutation | Accepted meaning, source, program, or human preference changes without a versioned record. | Use immutable versions, typed commands, receipts, and selective invalidation. |

**Stop conditions**

- The behavior would create a second semantic or canonical state owner.
- A required source, right, authority, contract, runtime, evaluator, or human decision is unavailable or unverified.
- The implementation would treat migration evidence or an external project as current authority.
- The change would imply real output, production readiness, or certification beyond available evidence.

## 10. Planning and implementation handoff

This module is implementation-ready only after its FRs have one primary vertical Story owner, its Stories pass CBAR hardening, its candidate Tech Specs identify exact existing code and target paths, and Program Control issues a bounded Development Capsule. Until then, this module is a product-authority draft.

*This feature module belongs to the Conscious Activations Atomic Harness Pipeline PRD V1.1 source-first reconciliation package.*


---

# F04 — Governed Retrieval and JIT Execution Capsule Compilation

## 1. Product claim and user outcome

**User outcome:** Every bounded decision receives the smallest constitutionally eligible and task-relevant context.

Combine deterministic eligibility, lexical/dense/graph/visual retrieval, contradiction coverage, and Minimum Complete Context into a receipt-bearing JIT Capsule. This feature exists to convert doctrine and source evidence into behavior that can be implemented, tested, denied, replayed, and audited. It does not grant implementation, provider, model-training, publication, production, or certification authority by itself.

## 2. Product boundary and ownership

The owning product is the Atomic Harness Pipeline unless an FR explicitly assigns Interview Expression, VAE, Delegation, Studio, Program Control, or an external runtime.

The feature must preserve the current product topology. Builder supplies the immutable Atomic Harness; Pipeline executes its declared nodes; Interview Expression owns source expression preparation and approval; VAE owns visual production; Delegation owns cross-product envelopes; Studio projects state and emits typed operator commands; Program Control owns cross-product authority and release truth. External renderers and models are embodiments, not sources of meaning.

## 3. Canonical objects and state

The feature consumes current, versioned upstream records and emits typed outputs that remain linked to the active Harness, source package where applicable, Workflow Node, JIT Capsule, execution binding, evaluator, and receipt. Canonical records use stable serialization and immutable identities. A UI projection, model response, provider job, renderer workspace, or local cache cannot become accepted product state until its contract and authority gates pass.

Core invariants for this feature are:

- Eligibility precedes ranking.
- Similarity never determines authority.
- Required contradictions, exclusions, and unavailable context remain visible.

## 4. Brownfield and external capability treatment

The implementation begins from exact current and predecessor evidence. The table below identifies the most relevant source records. `REUSE` or `ADAPT` permits bounded implementation reuse after namespace, authority, license, dependency, and behavior review; it never imports historical product meaning automatically.

| Source | Disposition | Exact path or reference | Role |
|---|---|---|---|
| `SRC-CUR-009` | `REFERENCE` | 01_ATOMIC_HARNESS_BUILDER/src/cmf_builder/skills/jit_capsule.py | Existing phase-local JIT Execution Capsule taxonomy and integrity rules. |
| `SRC-CUR-020` | `REFERENCE` | 02_VISUAL_ASSET_EDITOR/prd/05-features/F17-steering-intelligence-cmf-okf-retrieval.md | CMF-OKF, Steering Recipes, hybrid retrieval and Minimum Complete Context. |
| `SRC-EXT-005` | `REFERENCE` | https://huggingface.co/nvidia/Nemotron-3-Embed-1B-BF16 | Text/code dense retrieval candidate after deterministic eligibility filtering. |

## 5. Workflow integration

Validated upstream state → feature behavior → typed output and receipt → downstream handoff → evaluation, invalidation, and replay.

Every handoff is typed. A downstream node begins only after the producer output passes the declared contract and evidence gates. Failures are attributed to source, knowledge, retrieval, Skill, recipe, Programmed Model, tool, runtime, product, evaluator, or human-policy layers before repair or escalation.

## 6. Functional Requirements

### FR-019 — Declare node context requirements

**Lifecycle:** `PRESERVED_AND_DEEPENED`  
**Normative requirement:** Workflow Nodes shall declare typed context slots, authority, freshness, contradiction and budget requirements.

**Trigger and preconditions:** When a validated run, planning action, or operator request requires `Declare node context requirements` within feature F04.

**Required output or state transition:** A versioned, inspectable result or governed record that satisfies this requirement and can be consumed by the declared downstream owner.

**Authority and invariants:**
- Eligibility precedes ranking.
- Similarity never determines authority.
- Required contradictions, exclusions, and unavailable context remain visible.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given current authority, valid inputs, and an eligible execution binding, when this behavior runs, then workflow Nodes shall declare typed context slots, authority, freshness, contradiction and budget requirements and the downstream consumer receives a contract-valid result.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given stale, ineligible, ambiguous, out-of-scope, or unverifiable inputs, when this behavior is requested, then no unauthorized side effect occurs and a typed blocker names the cause, owner, and next admissible action.
- **Evidence required:** retrieval benchmark, hard-negative tests, context-size reduction, downstream decision lift, and receipts, linked to an immutable requirement receipt.

**Governing decisions:** D013, D014, D015, D016, D017, D034  
**Exact source references:** SRC-CUR-009, SRC-CUR-020, SRC-EXT-005

# F05 — Durable State, Checkpoints, Replay, Cancellation, and Recovery

## 1. Product claim and user outcome

**User outcome:** Long-running multi-product work remains resumable, cancelable, attributable, and recoverable without repeating accepted work.

Persist immutable events and atomic state transitions while separating resume, replay, repair, retry, cancellation, backup, and restore. This feature exists to convert doctrine and source evidence into behavior that can be implemented, tested, denied, replayed, and audited. It does not grant implementation, provider, model-training, publication, production, or certification authority by itself.

## 2. Product boundary and ownership

The owning product is the Atomic Harness Pipeline unless an FR explicitly assigns Interview Expression, VAE, Delegation, Studio, Program Control, or an external runtime.

The feature must preserve the current product topology. Builder supplies the immutable Atomic Harness; Pipeline executes its declared nodes; Interview Expression owns source expression preparation and approval; VAE owns visual production; Delegation owns cross-product envelopes; Studio projects state and emits typed operator commands; Program Control owns cross-product authority and release truth. External renderers and models are embodiments, not sources of meaning.

## 3. Canonical objects and state

The feature consumes current, versioned upstream records and emits typed outputs that remain linked to the active Harness, source package where applicable, Workflow Node, JIT Capsule, execution binding, evaluator, and receipt. Canonical records use stable serialization and immutable identities. A UI projection, model response, provider job, renderer workspace, or local cache cannot become accepted product state until its contract and authority gates pass.

Core invariants for this feature are:

- State and receipt commit atomically.
- Accepted checkpoints require validation.
- Late results and migrations preserve history.

## 4. Brownfield and external capability treatment

The implementation begins from exact current and predecessor evidence. The table below identifies the most relevant source records. `REUSE` or `ADAPT` permits bounded implementation reuse after namespace, authority, license, dependency, and behavior review; it never imports historical product meaning automatically.

| Source | Disposition | Exact path or reference | Role |
|---|---|---|---|
| `SRC-CUR-010` | `REFERENCE` | 01_ATOMIC_HARNESS_BUILDER/src/cmf_builder/workflow/actor_explicit_contracts.py | Execution-free Workflow Node, edge, authority and validation contracts. |
| `SRC-CUR-017` | `REFERENCE` | 02_VISUAL_ASSET_EDITOR/prd/05-features/F10-event-sourced-production-runtime.md | Event-sourced VAE production runtime. |
| `SRC-LEG-002` | `ADAPT` | src/ccp_studio/services/pipeline_run_service.py | Reuse run-state behavior after durable-state and receipt reconciliation. |
| `SRC-LEG-003` | `ADAPT` | src/ccp_studio/services/pipeline_step_run_service.py | Map legacy steps to current Workflow Nodes. |

| Risk | Concrete consequence | Mitigation |
|---|---|---|
| Authority drift | A predecessor, external project, UI, model, or renderer is treated as current product authority. | Require exact source disposition, current authority validation, and product-boundary tests. |
| False completion | A synthetic URI, dry-run, unverified command, or model self-report is promoted as a real result. | Require actual files, hashes, independent validation, and artifact-class labels. |
| Over-broad automation | A model or agent gains tools, context, or authority beyond the current node. | Use JIT context, node-local tool grants, sandboxes, and explicit escalation. |
| Hidden mutation | Accepted meaning, source, program, or human preference changes without a versioned record. | Use immutable versions, typed commands, receipts, and selective invalidation. |

**Stop conditions**

- The behavior would create a second semantic or canonical state owner.
- A required source, right, authority, contract, runtime, evaluator, or human decision is unavailable or unverified.
- The implementation would treat migration evidence or an external project as current authority.
- The change would imply real output, production readiness, or certification beyond available evidence.

## 10. Planning and implementation handoff

This module is implementation-ready only after its FRs have one primary vertical Story owner, its Stories pass CBAR hardening, its candidate Tech Specs identify exact existing code and target paths, and Program Control issues a bounded Development Capsule. Until then, this module is a product-authority draft.

*This feature module belongs to the Conscious Activations Atomic Harness Pipeline PRD V1.1 source-first reconciliation package.*

# F06 — Skills, Skill Composition Recipes, Steering Recipes, and Transformation Contracts

## 1. Product claim and user outcome

**User outcome:** Stable behavior, conditional strategy, current context, and execution-specific bindings remain separate and inspectable.

Let Atomic Harnesses activate reusable Skills and evidence-backed Steering Recipes without embedding mutable truth or collapsing taste into prompts. This feature exists to convert doctrine and source evidence into behavior that can be implemented, tested, denied, replayed, and audited. It does not grant implementation, provider, model-training, publication, production, or certification authority by itself.

## 2. Product boundary and ownership

The owning product is the Atomic Harness Pipeline unless an FR explicitly assigns Interview Expression, VAE, Delegation, Studio, Program Control, or an external runtime.

The feature must preserve the current product topology. Builder supplies the immutable Atomic Harness; Pipeline executes its declared nodes; Interview Expression owns source expression preparation and approval; VAE owns visual production; Delegation owns cross-product envelopes; Studio projects state and emits typed operator commands; Program Control owns cross-product authority and release truth. External renderers and models are embodiments, not sources of meaning.

## 3. Canonical objects and state

The feature consumes current, versioned upstream records and emits typed outputs that remain linked to the active Harness, source package where applicable, Workflow Node, JIT Capsule, execution binding, evaluator, and receipt. Canonical records use stable serialization and immutable identities. A UI projection, model response, provider job, renderer workspace, or local cache cannot become accepted product state until its contract and authority gates pass.

Core invariants for this feature are:

- Canonical Skills are not mutated by local adaptations.
- Recipes carry applicability and lifecycle.
- Transformation Contracts protect meaning while declaring creative freedom.

## 4. Brownfield and external capability treatment

The implementation begins from exact current and predecessor evidence. The table below identifies the most relevant source records. `REUSE` or `ADAPT` permits bounded implementation reuse after namespace, authority, license, dependency, and behavior review; it never imports historical product meaning automatically.

| Source | Disposition | Exact path or reference | Role |
|---|---|---|---|
| `SRC-CUR-009` | `REFERENCE` | 01_ATOMIC_HARNESS_BUILDER/src/cmf_builder/skills/jit_capsule.py | Existing phase-local JIT Execution Capsule taxonomy and integrity rules. |
| `SRC-CUR-020` | `REFERENCE` | 02_VISUAL_ASSET_EDITOR/prd/05-features/F17-steering-intelligence-cmf-okf-retrieval.md | CMF-OKF, Steering Recipes, hybrid retrieval and Minimum Complete Context. |

## 5. Workflow integration

Validated upstream state → feature behavior → typed output and receipt → downstream handoff → evaluation, invalidation, and replay.

Every handoff is typed. A downstream node begins only after the producer output passes the declared contract and evidence gates. Failures are attributed to source, knowledge, retrieval, Skill, recipe, Programmed Model, tool, runtime, product, evaluator, or human-policy layers before repair or escalation.

## 6. Functional Requirements

### FR-031 — Bind Canonical Skills explicitly

**Lifecycle:** `PRESERVED_AND_DEEPENED`  
**Normative requirement:** A learned or agentic Workflow Node shall reference the exact Canonical Skill governing its stable procedure.

**Trigger and preconditions:** When a validated run, planning action, or operator request requires `Bind Canonical Skills explicitly` within feature F06.

**Required output or state transition:** A versioned, inspectable result or governed record that satisfies this requirement and can be consumed by the declared downstream owner.

**Authority and invariants:**
- Canonical Skills are not mutated by local adaptations.
- Recipes carry applicability and lifecycle.
- Transformation Contracts protect meaning while declaring creative freedom.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given current authority, valid inputs, and an eligible execution binding, when this behavior runs, then a learned or agentic Workflow Node shall reference the exact Canonical Skill governing its stable procedure and the downstream consumer receives a contract-valid result.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given stale, ineligible, ambiguous, out-of-scope, or unverifiable inputs, when this behavior is requested, then no unauthorized side effect occurs and a typed blocker names the cause, owner, and next admissible action.
- **Evidence required:** skill/recipe binding tests, eligibility/exclusion, recipe lifecycle, transformation validation, and retrieval receipts, linked to an immutable requirement receipt.

**Governing decisions:** D007, D016, D019, D023, D024, D026  
**Exact source references:** SRC-CUR-009, SRC-CUR-020

## 7. Execution, model, tool, and human responsibilities

Deterministic services own mechanically decidable facts. Programmed Models or bounded Agent Programs may propose or compile behavior only within their evidence-backed claim and node-local tool grants. Independent evaluators inspect judgment dimensions. Humans own new meaning, consent, identity, unresolved taste, policy exceptions, promotion, and publication authority where assigned. The producing model or runtime cannot accept its own output.

When the feature uses a Hunter, Analyst, Composer, or Commander role, the role is an explicit workflow responsibility. It may be implemented by code, a small model, a larger model, or a human. The role name never hides the actual actor or expand its authority.

## 8. Validation and quality gates

Validation must prove both the intended result and the process that produced it. The minimum feature evidence includes skill/recipe binding tests, eligibility/exclusion, recipe lifecycle, transformation validation, and retrieval receipts. Mechanical tests run before expensive model or visual evaluation. Judgment evaluators are calibrated to the exact category and context. Every denial names the cause, owner, and next admissible action. Every accepted mutation emits an immutable receipt and updates only dependent state.

## 9. Risks, mitigations, and stop conditions

| Risk | Concrete consequence | Mitigation |
|---|---|---|
| Authority drift | A predecessor, external project, UI, model, or renderer is treated as current product authority. | Require exact source disposition, current authority validation, and product-boundary tests. |
| False completion | A synthetic URI, dry-run, unverified command, or model self-report is promoted as a real result. | Require actual files, hashes, independent validation, and artifact-class labels. |
| Over-broad automation | A model or agent gains tools, context, or authority beyond the current node. | Use JIT context, node-local tool grants, sandboxes, and explicit escalation. |
| Hidden mutation | Accepted meaning, source, program, or human preference changes without a versioned record. | Use immutable versions, typed commands, receipts, and selective invalidation. |

**Stop conditions**

- The behavior would create a second semantic or canonical state owner.
- A required source, right, authority, contract, runtime, evaluator, or human decision is unavailable or unverified.
- The implementation would treat migration evidence or an external project as current authority.
- The change would imply real output, production readiness, or certification beyond available evidence.

| Authority drift | A predecessor, external project, UI, model, or renderer is treated as current product authority. | Require exact source disposition, current authority validation, and product-boundary tests. |
| False completion | A synthetic URI, dry-run, unverified command, or model self-report is promoted as a real result. | Require actual files, hashes, independent validation, and artifact-class labels. |
| Over-broad automation | A model or agent gains tools, context, or authority beyond the current node. | Use JIT context, node-local tool grants, sandboxes, and explicit escalation. |
| Hidden mutation | Accepted meaning, source, program, or human preference changes without a versioned record. | Use immutable versions, typed commands, receipts, and selective invalidation. |

**Stop conditions**

- The behavior would create a second semantic or canonical state owner.
- A required source, right, authority, contract, runtime, evaluator, or human decision is unavailable or unverified.
- The implementation would treat migration evidence or an external project as current authority.
- The change would imply real output, production readiness, or certification beyond available evidence.

## 10. Planning and implementation handoff

This module is implementation-ready only after its FRs have one primary vertical Story owner, its Stories pass CBAR hardening, its candidate Tech Specs identify exact existing code and target paths, and Program Control issues a bounded Development Capsule. Until then, this module is a product-authority draft.

*This feature module belongs to the Conscious Activations Atomic Harness Pipeline PRD V1.1 source-first reconciliation package.*

# F08 — Adaptive Candidate Search and Comparative Selection

## 1. Product claim and user outcome

**User outcome:** The Pipeline obtains strong results through purposeful diversity and independent comparison rather than blind repetition.

Select candidate-search policy per claim, enforce meaningful diversity and mechanical filters, and stop by evidence and budget. This feature exists to convert doctrine and source evidence into behavior that can be implemented, tested, denied, replayed, and audited. It does not grant implementation, provider, model-training, publication, production, or certification authority by itself.

## 2. Product boundary and ownership

The owning product is the Atomic Harness Pipeline unless an FR explicitly assigns Interview Expression, VAE, Delegation, Studio, Program Control, or an external runtime.

The feature must preserve the current product topology. Builder supplies the immutable Atomic Harness; Pipeline executes its declared nodes; Interview Expression owns source expression preparation and approval; VAE owns visual production; Delegation owns cross-product envelopes; Studio projects state and emits typed operator commands; Program Control owns cross-product authority and release truth. External renderers and models are embodiments, not sources of meaning.

## 3. Canonical objects and state

The feature consumes current, versioned upstream records and emits typed outputs that remain linked to the active Harness, source package where applicable, Workflow Node, JIT Capsule, execution binding, evaluator, and receipt. Canonical records use stable serialization and immutable identities. A UI projection, model response, provider job, renderer workspace, or local cache cannot become accepted product state until its contract and authority gates pass.

Core invariants for this feature are:

- Invalid candidates are removed before comparison.
- Producer and evaluator are independent.
- Search stops rather than looping.

## 4. Brownfield and external capability treatment

The implementation begins from exact current and predecessor evidence. The table below identifies the most relevant source records. `REUSE` or `ADAPT` permits bounded implementation reuse after namespace, authority, license, dependency, and behavior review; it never imports historical product meaning automatically.

| Source | Disposition | Exact path or reference | Role |
|---|---|---|---|
| `SRC-CUR-018` | `REFERENCE` | 02_VISUAL_ASSET_EDITOR/prd/05-features/F14-visual-evaluation-profiles.md | Independent visual evaluation profiles. |
| `SRC-EXT-001` | `REFERENCE` | file:///mnt/data/Agentic Prompt Enhancer for Image Generation and.pdf | Trainable small prompt enhancers; router–rewriter–composer and downstream-output reward. |

## 5. Workflow integration

Validated upstream state → feature behavior → typed output and receipt → downstream handoff → evaluation, invalidation, and replay.

Every handoff is typed. A downstream node begins only after the producer output passes the declared contract and evidence gates. Failures are attributed to source, knowledge, retrieval, Skill, recipe, Programmed Model, tool, runtime, product, evaluator, or human-policy layers before repair or escalation.

## 6. Functional Requirements

### FR-043 — Declare candidate-search policy per claim

**Lifecycle:** `PRESERVED_AND_DEEPENED`

**Trigger and preconditions:** When a validated run, planning action, or operator request requires `Declare candidate-search policy per claim` within feature F08.

**Required output or state transition:** A versioned, inspectable result or governed record that satisfies this requirement and can be consumed by the declared downstream owner.

**Authority and invariants:**
- Invalid candidates are removed before comparison.
- Producer and evaluator are independent.
- Search stops rather than looping.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given current authority, valid inputs, and an eligible execution binding, when this behavior runs, then a learned claim shall specify single-candidate, draft/revise or best-of-N behavior and its evidence basis and the downstream consumer receives a contract-valid result.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given stale, ineligible, ambiguous, out-of-scope, or unverifiable inputs, when this behavior is requested, then no unauthorized side effect occurs and a typed blocker names the cause, owner, and next admissible action.
- **Evidence required:** candidate diversity metrics, budget/stop tests, comparative evaluation, and portfolio learning, linked to an immutable requirement receipt.

## 7. Execution, model, tool, and human responsibilities

Deterministic services own mechanically decidable facts. Programmed Models or bounded Agent Programs may propose or compile behavior only within their evidence-backed claim and node-local tool grants. Independent evaluators inspect judgment dimensions. Humans own new meaning, consent, identity, unresolved taste, policy exceptions, promotion, and publication authority where assigned. The producing model or runtime cannot accept its own output.

When the feature uses a Hunter, Analyst, Composer, or Commander role, the role is an explicit workflow responsibility. It may be implemented by code, a small model, a larger model, or a human. The role name never hides the actual actor or expand its authority.

## 8. Validation and quality gates

Validation must prove both the intended result and the process that produced it. The minimum feature evidence includes candidate diversity metrics, budget/stop tests, comparative evaluation, and portfolio learning. Mechanical tests run before expensive model or visual evaluation. Judgment evaluators are calibrated to the exact category and context. Every denial names the cause, owner, and next admissible action. Every accepted mutation emits an immutable receipt and updates only dependent state.

## 9. Risks, mitigations, and stop conditions

| Risk | Concrete consequence | Mitigation |
|---|---|---|
| Authority drift | A predecessor, external project, UI, model, or renderer is treated as current product authority. | Require exact source disposition, current authority validation, and product-boundary tests. |
| False completion | A synthetic URI, dry-run, unverified command, or model self-report is promoted as a real result. | Require actual files, hashes, independent validation, and artifact-class labels. |
| Over-broad automation | A model or agent gains tools, context, or authority beyond the current node. | Use JIT context, node-local tool grants, sandboxes, and explicit escalation. |
| Hidden mutation | Accepted meaning, source, program, or human preference changes without a versioned record. | Use immutable versions, typed commands, receipts, and selective invalidation. |

**Stop conditions**

- The behavior would create a second semantic or canonical state owner.
- A required source, right, authority, contract, runtime, evaluator, or human decision is unavailable or unverified.
- The implementation would treat migration evidence or an external project as current authority.
- The change would imply real output, production readiness, or certification beyond available evidence.

| Authority drift | A predecessor, external project, UI, model, or renderer is treated as current product authority. | Require exact source disposition, current authority validation, and product-boundary tests. |
| False completion | A synthetic URI, dry-run, unverified command, or model self-report is promoted as a real result. | Require actual files, hashes, independent validation, and artifact-class labels. |
| Over-broad automation | A model or agent gains tools, context, or authority beyond the current node. | Use JIT context, node-local tool grants, sandboxes, and explicit escalation. |
| Hidden mutation | Accepted meaning, source, program, or human preference changes without a versioned record. | Use immutable versions, typed commands, receipts, and selective invalidation. |

**Stop conditions**

- The behavior would create a second semantic or canonical state owner.
- A required source, right, authority, contract, runtime, evaluator, or human decision is unavailable or unverified.
- The implementation would treat migration evidence or an external project as current authority.
- The change would imply real output, production readiness, or certification beyond available evidence.

## 10. Planning and implementation handoff

This module is implementation-ready only after its FRs have one primary vertical Story owner, its Stories pass CBAR hardening, its candidate Tech Specs identify exact existing code and target paths, and Program Control issues a bounded Development Capsule. Until then, this module is a product-authority draft.

*This feature module belongs to the Conscious Activations Atomic Harness Pipeline PRD V1.1 source-first reconciliation package.*


---

# F10 — Carousel Category Runtime

## 1. Product claim and user outcome

**User outcome:** Carousel execution preserves source-backed slide grammar, swipe progression, and cross-slide continuity.

Compile source ingredients and Activative sequence into slide-native roles and deterministic export packages after profile ratification. This feature exists to convert doctrine and source evidence into behavior that can be implemented, tested, denied, replayed, and audited. It does not grant implementation, provider, model-training, publication, production, or certification authority by itself.

## 2. Product boundary and ownership

The owning product is the Atomic Harness Pipeline unless an FR explicitly assigns Interview Expression, VAE, Delegation, Studio, Program Control, or an external runtime.

The feature must preserve the current product topology. Builder supplies the immutable Atomic Harness; Pipeline executes its declared nodes; Interview Expression owns source expression preparation and approval; VAE owns visual production; Delegation owns cross-product envelopes; Studio projects state and emits typed operator commands; Program Control owns cross-product authority and release truth. External renderers and models are embodiments, not sources of meaning.

## 3. Canonical objects and state

The feature consumes current, versioned upstream records and emits typed outputs that remain linked to the active Harness, source package where applicable, Workflow Node, JIT Capsule, execution binding, evaluator, and receipt. Canonical records use stable serialization and immutable identities. A UI projection, model response, provider job, renderer workspace, or local cache cannot become accepted product state until its contract and authority gates pass.

Core invariants for this feature are:

- Carousel is not flattened into frame-time motion.
- Profiles require current authority.
- Every claim and quote preserves source/evidence lineage.

## 4. Brownfield and external capability treatment

The implementation begins from exact current and predecessor evidence. The table below identifies the most relevant source records. `REUSE` or `ADAPT` permits bounded implementation reuse after namespace, authority, license, dependency, and behavior review; it never imports historical product meaning automatically.

| Source | Disposition | Exact path or reference | Role |
|---|---|---|---|
| `SRC-CUR-007` | `REFERENCE` | 01_ATOMIC_HARNESS_BUILDER/src/cmf_builder/domain/category_runtime_rules.py | Category-native runtime plan requirements, evaluation dimensions and repair units. |
| `SRC-LEG-024` | `FORK_ADAPT` | src/ccp_studio/services/carousel_engine_service.py | Map to current Carousel category laws and future ratified format profiles. |
| `SRC-LEG-025` | `REPLACE_ACTIVATE` | src/ccp_studio/services/carousel_render_service.py | Replace synthetic references with actual Skia artifacts. |
| `SRC-LEG-037` | `RETAIN_AND_ADAPT` | docs/tech-specs/TS-CMF-096-carousel-slide-composition-library-and-sequence-builder.md | Carousel sequence specification. |
| `SRC-LEG-038` | `RETAIN_AND_ADAPT` | docs/tech-specs/TS-CMF-097-carousel-builder-engine-compiler-workflow-and-skia-export-runtime.md | Carousel compiler and Skia export specification. |
| `SRC-LEG-039` | `RETAIN_AS_CANDIDATE_EVIDENCE` | docs/tech-specs/TS-CMF-098-carousel-composition-atlas-registry-and-router-integration.md | Candidate profile and training/benchmark evidence only. |

## 5. Workflow integration

Validated upstream state → feature behavior → typed output and receipt → downstream handoff → evaluation, invalidation, and replay.

Every handoff is typed. A downstream node begins only after the producer output passes the declared contract and evidence gates. Failures are attributed to source, knowledge, retrieval, Skill, recipe, Programmed Model, tool, runtime, product, evaluator, or human-policy layers before repair or escalation.

## 6. Functional Requirements

### FR-055 — Enforce Carousel Category identity

**Lifecycle:** `PRESERVED_AND_DEEPENED`  
**Normative requirement:** Carousel plans shall reject frame-time motion semantics and cross-category profile reuse.

**Trigger and preconditions:** When a validated run, planning action, or operator request requires `Enforce Carousel Category identity` within feature F10.

**Required output or state transition:** A versioned, inspectable result or governed record that satisfies this requirement and can be consumed by the declared downstream owner.

**Authority and invariants:**
- Carousel is not flattened into frame-time motion.
- Profiles require current authority.
- Every claim and quote preserves source/evidence lineage.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given current authority, valid inputs, and an eligible execution binding, when this behavior runs, then carousel plans shall reject frame-time motion semantics and cross-category profile reuse and the downstream consumer receives a contract-valid result.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given stale, ineligible, ambiguous, out-of-scope, or unverifiable inputs, when this behavior is requested, then no unauthorized side effect occurs and a typed blocker names the cause, owner, and next admissible action.
- **Evidence required:** slide/source traceability, sequence evaluation, cross-slide continuity, export manifests, and profile authority, linked to an immutable requirement receipt.

**Governing decisions:** D023, D027, D028, D029, D039

## 7. Execution, model, tool, and human responsibilities

Deterministic services own mechanically decidable facts. Programmed Models or bounded Agent Programs may propose or compile behavior only within their evidence-backed claim and node-local tool grants. Independent evaluators inspect judgment dimensions. Humans own new meaning, consent, identity, unresolved taste, policy exceptions, promotion, and publication authority where assigned. The producing model or runtime cannot accept its own output.

When the feature uses a Hunter, Analyst, Composer, or Commander role, the role is an explicit workflow responsibility. It may be implemented by code, a small model, a larger model, or a human. The role name never hides the actual actor or expand its authority.

## 8. Validation and quality gates

Validation must prove both the intended result and the process that produced it. The minimum feature evidence includes slide/source traceability, sequence evaluation, cross-slide continuity, export manifests, and profile authority. Mechanical tests run before expensive model or visual evaluation. Judgment evaluators are calibrated to the exact category and context. Every denial names the cause, owner, and next admissible action. Every accepted mutation emits an immutable receipt and updates only dependent state.

## 9. Risks, mitigations, and stop conditions

| Risk | Concrete consequence | Mitigation |
|---|---|---|
| Authority drift | A predecessor, external project, UI, model, or renderer is treated as current product authority. | Require exact source disposition, current authority validation, and product-boundary tests. |
| False completion | A synthetic URI, dry-run, unverified command, or model self-report is promoted as a real result. | Require actual files, hashes, independent validation, and artifact-class labels. |
| Over-broad automation | A model or agent gains tools, context, or authority beyond the current node. | Use JIT context, node-local tool grants, sandboxes, and explicit escalation. |
| Hidden mutation | Accepted meaning, source, program, or human preference changes without a versioned record. | Use immutable versions, typed commands, receipts, and selective invalidation. |

**Stop conditions**

- The behavior would create a second semantic or canonical state owner.
- A required source, right, authority, contract, runtime, evaluator, or human decision is unavailable or unverified.
- The implementation would treat migration evidence or an external project as current authority.
- The change would imply real output, production readiness, or certification beyond available evidence.

## 10. Planning and implementation handoff

This module is implementation-ready only after its FRs have one primary vertical Story owner, its Stories pass CBAR hardening, its candidate Tech Specs identify exact existing code and target paths, and Program Control issues a bounded Development Capsule. Until then, this module is a product-authority draft.

*This feature module belongs to the Conscious Activations Atomic Harness Pipeline PRD V1.1 source-first reconciliation package.*

- A required source, right, authority, contract, runtime, evaluator, or human decision is unavailable or unverified.
- The implementation would treat migration evidence or an external project as current authority.
- The change would imply real output, production readiness, or certification beyond available evidence.

## 10. Planning and implementation handoff

This module is implementation-ready only after its FRs have one primary vertical Story owner, its Stories pass CBAR hardening, its candidate Tech Specs identify exact existing code and target paths, and Program Control issues a bounded Development Capsule. Until then, this module is a product-authority draft.

*This feature module belongs to the Conscious Activations Atomic Harness Pipeline PRD V1.1 source-first reconciliation package.*

# F12 — Source-First Short-Form Video Editing and Adopted Timeline Runtime

## 1. Product claim and user outcome

**User outcome:** Interview-derived shorts preserve talking-head A-roll as the base timeline and automate word-safe, source-grounded editing through a canonical VideoEditProgram.

Adopt predecessor edit/timeline contracts, bind source spans, support layers, and temporal embodiments, and keep the UI as a projection and command surface. This feature exists to convert doctrine and source evidence into behavior that can be implemented, tested, denied, replayed, and audited. It does not grant implementation, provider, model-training, publication, production, or certification authority by itself.

## 2. Product boundary and ownership

The owning product is the Atomic Harness Pipeline unless an FR explicitly assigns Interview Expression, VAE, Delegation, Studio, Program Control, or an external runtime.

The feature must preserve the current product topology. Builder supplies the immutable Atomic Harness; Pipeline executes its declared nodes; Interview Expression owns source expression preparation and approval; VAE owns visual production; Delegation owns cross-product envelopes; Studio projects state and emits typed operator commands; Program Control owns cross-product authority and release truth. External renderers and models are embodiments, not sources of meaning.

## 3. Canonical objects and state

The feature consumes current, versioned upstream records and emits typed outputs that remain linked to the active Harness, source package where applicable, Workflow Node, JIT Capsule, execution binding, evaluator, and receipt. Canonical records use stable serialization and immutable identities. A UI projection, model response, provider job, renderer workspace, or local cache cannot become accepted product state until its contract and authority gates pass.

Core invariants for this feature are:

- Original talking-head footage remains the A-roll spine.
- No second timeline truth exists.
- Every cut and layer preserves source/function lineage.

## 4. Brownfield and external capability treatment

The implementation begins from exact current and predecessor evidence. The table below identifies the most relevant source records. `REUSE` or `ADAPT` permits bounded implementation reuse after namespace, authority, license, dependency, and behavior review; it never imports historical product meaning automatically.
