## 5. Workflow integration

Validated upstream state → feature behavior → typed output and receipt → downstream handoff → evaluation, invalidation, and replay.

Every handoff is typed. A downstream node begins only after the producer output passes the declared contract and evidence gates. Failures are attributed to source, knowledge, retrieval, Skill, recipe, Programmed Model, tool, runtime, product, evaluator, or human-policy layers before repair or escalation.

## 6. Functional Requirements

### FR-067 — Adopt the existing VideoEditProgram and timeline contracts

**Lifecycle:** `AMENDED_V1_1`  
**Normative requirement:** The Pipeline shall adopt and normalize the predecessor CMF edit-decision and timeline contracts as the canonical temporal editing program, extending them for current source lineage, Activative sequence, Transformation Contracts, runtime bindings, evaluation, and selective repair rather than creating a second timeline model.

**Trigger and preconditions:** An edited-video Atomic Harness reaches temporal planning with an accepted Canonical Interview Source Package and source-backed sequence purpose.

**Required output or state transition:** A versioned VideoEditProgram containing source spans, output-time mapping, tracks, captions, audio, visual treatments, runtime bindings, evaluation requirements, and exact lineage.

**Authority and invariants:**
- No second timeline truth is introduced.
- The UI remains a projection and command surface.
- Source meaning and approved span lineage cannot be changed by renderer adapters.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given a valid interview source package and Harness sequence, when the temporal program is compiled, then every program element resolves to an existing source, approved derivative, or typed generated slot and can be reconstructed after reload.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given an implementation that stores hidden timeline state only inside a browser component, when the project is reopened, then admission fails because the canonical program cannot be reproduced.
- **Evidence required:** Canonical serialized program, migration mapping from predecessor contracts, schema validation, round-trip test, and source-lineage receipt.

**Governing decisions:** D023, D027, D028, D029, D030, D035, D043, D049, D053  
**Exact source references:** SRC-CUR-007, SRC-LEG-006, SRC-LEG-007, SRC-LEG-008, SRC-LEG-009, SRC-LEG-010, SRC-LEG-011, SRC-LEG-012, SRC-AM-001, SRC-EXT-017, SRC-EXT-018, SRC-EXT-019


### FR-068 — Register canonical interview source media

**Lifecycle:** `AMENDED_V1_1`  
**Normative requirement:** The temporal runtime shall ingest source media only through an accepted Canonical Interview Source Package, verify immutable file identities and technical metadata, and expose source-time ranges without mutating the originals.

**Trigger and preconditions:** A source package is admitted for a short-video job.

**Required output or state transition:** Source asset records, ffprobe metadata, time bases, audio streams, shot map, transcript alignment, keyframe references, and immutable source hashes.

**Authority and invariants:**
- Original source bytes remain untouched.
- All derivative timestamps use declared source time bases.
- Missing or unverifiable source files block execution.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given an uploaded interview and transcript, when intake completes, then the runtime can resolve every transcript word and candidate span to the exact source file and time range.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given a transcript whose duration or source identity cannot be reconciled with the video, when admission runs, then no edit decision is accepted and a typed alignment blocker is issued.
- **Evidence required:** Media probe receipt, hash ledger, transcript alignment report, shot/keyframe index, and source-package acceptance receipt.

**Governing decisions:** D023, D027, D043, D044, D054  
**Exact source references:** SRC-INT-001, SRC-INT-002, SRC-INT-003, SRC-AM-002, SRC-EXT-017, SRC-EXT-020, SRC-EXT-023


### FR-069 — Compile source-backed A-roll edit decisions

**Lifecycle:** `AMENDED_V1_1`  
**Normative requirement:** Every selected A-roll span, cut, hold, reorder, reaction extension, and transition shall preserve exact source-time lineage, land on valid word or audio-event boundaries where required, declare its narrative or Activative function, and map deterministically into output time.

**Trigger and preconditions:** A short-video Harness has an approved source expression sequence and target duration.

**Required output or state transition:** A-roll EDL entries with source ID, source start/end, output start/end, transcript phrase/word refs, speaker, beat/archetype role, cut padding, and reason.

**Authority and invariants:**
- No cut occurs inside a protected word.
- Reactions, laughter, sighs, and expression tails are not removed without an explicit decision.
- Source order changes remain inspectable.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given an approved Expression Moment, when the A-roll compiler creates a short, then the result begins and ends on permitted source boundaries and the output duration is recomputable from the EDL.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given a proposed cut through a word or an unsupported paraphrase represented as source speech, when validation runs, then the EDL is rejected before rendering.
- **Evidence required:** Word-boundary validation, source/output time map, EDL hash, phrase references, and cut-purpose receipt.

**Governing decisions:** D023, D027, D043, D044, D052, D053  
**Exact source references:** SRC-AM-002, SRC-EXT-017, SRC-EXT-020, SRC-EXT-023, SRC-EXT-024, SRC-LEG-006, SRC-LEG-007


### FR-070 — Compile captions, audio, evidence, and motion support around A-roll

**Lifecycle:** `AMENDED_V1_1`  
**Normative requirement:** The edit program shall compile exact captions, audio treatment, color, reframing, B-roll, evidence inserts, keyframe freezes, designed overlays, annotation cues, and bounded animation slots as supporting layers around the talking-head A-roll spine.

**Trigger and preconditions:** The A-roll EDL is accepted and the Harness declares supporting visual or audio functions.

**Required output or state transition:** Typed track/layer records, caption plan, audio mix plan, B-roll/evidence slots, motion-block requests, composition constraints, and child-runtime bindings.

**Authority and invariants:**
- Supporting layers cannot contradict or replace source truth.
- Captions preserve verbatim source words unless explicitly marked as editorial text.
- Every insert has a declared function and lineage.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given a claim with supporting evidence, when a proof card is inserted, then it is timed to the source statement, cites its evidence object, respects face/caption safe regions, and returns to A-roll without losing source continuity.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given an attractive generated overlay with no declared function or evidence, when program validation runs, then it is excluded from the accepted edit program.
- **Evidence required:** Track manifest, caption word map, audio plan, motion-slot receipts, B-roll/evidence lineage, and composition preview.

**Governing decisions:** D023, D027, D043, D044, D053  
**Exact source references:** SRC-EXT-017, SRC-EXT-018, SRC-EXT-019, SRC-EXT-021, SRC-EXT-022, SRC-LEG-008, SRC-LEG-009, SRC-LEG-010


### FR-071 — Bind temporal embodiments explicitly

**Lifecycle:** `AMENDED_V1_1`  
**Normative requirement:** Remotion, HyperFrames, FFmpeg, Stretchy/Spine, or another approved temporal embodiment shall be selected through an immutable compatibility and authority decision; child renderers may realize bounded slots but may not silently replace the master edit program or each other.

**Trigger and preconditions:** A validated VideoEditProgram requires one or more renderer capabilities.

**Required output or state transition:** A runtime binding manifest identifying master compositor, child slots, versions, dependencies, fallback policy, and expected artifacts.

**Authority and invariants:**
- No silent renderer substitution.
- Renderer selection does not change semantic or composition authority.
- License and capability eligibility precede execution.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given a Remotion master timeline and a HyperFrames motion slot, when rendering starts, then both exact bindings are recorded and the HyperFrames output is consumed only at its declared slot.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given an unavailable Remotion binding, when the fallback is not explicitly authorized, then the system blocks rather than switching to a different compositor.
- **Evidence required:** Binding decision, compatibility report, runtime health check, license disposition, and resolved execution fingerprint.

**Governing decisions:** D023, D027, D049, D053  
**Exact source references:** SRC-EXT-018, SRC-EXT-019, SRC-EXT-025, SRC-LEG-013, SRC-LEG-014, SRC-LEG-015


### FR-072 — Enforce FFmpeg production-correctness rules

**Lifecycle:** `AMENDED_V1_1`  
**Normative requirement:** FFmpeg shall be a first-class media engine for probe, lossless extraction where eligible, trim, concat, audio fades, retime, filters, grade, mix, subtitle composition, mux, encode, and delivery validation under versioned production-correctness rules.

**Trigger and preconditions:** The accepted VideoEditProgram requires source extraction, media transformation, finishing, or export.

**Required output or state transition:** Intermediate media segments, final encoded files, command manifests, technical QA, and process receipts.

**Authority and invariants:**
- Cut boundaries receive declared audio treatment.
- Subtitle timing uses output-time mapping.
- No successful result is inferred from a command string or synthetic URI.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given a multi-segment A-roll EDL, when FFmpeg finishing executes, then the output has no audible boundary pops, captions align after concat, and ffprobe matches the expected duration, codec, dimensions, and streams.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given a render command that exits without producing the declared file or whose probe differs from the plan, when validation runs, then the job fails and no production artifact is promoted.
- **Evidence required:** Executed command receipt, binary/version identity, output hash, ffprobe report, boundary checks, and caption/audio validation.

**Governing decisions:** D023, D027, D053  
**Exact source references:** SRC-EXT-017, SRC-EXT-018, SRC-LEG-011, SRC-LEG-012


## 7. Execution, model, tool, and human responsibilities

Deterministic services own mechanically decidable facts. Programmed Models or bounded Agent Programs may propose or compile behavior only within their evidence-backed claim and node-local tool grants. Independent evaluators inspect judgment dimensions. Humans own new meaning, consent, identity, unresolved taste, policy exceptions, promotion, and publication authority where assigned. The producing model or runtime cannot accept its own output.

When the feature uses a Hunter, Analyst, Composer, or Commander role, the role is an explicit workflow responsibility. It may be implemented by code, a small model, a larger model, or a human. The role name never hides the actual actor or expand its authority.

## 8. Validation and quality gates

Validation must prove both the intended result and the process that produced it. The minimum feature evidence includes source/time maps, EDL validation, round-trip/reload tests, runtime bindings, FFmpeg correctness, and rendered boundary evaluation. Mechanical tests run before expensive model or visual evaluation. Judgment evaluators are calibrated to the exact category and context. Every denial names the cause, owner, and next admissible action. Every accepted mutation emits an immutable receipt and updates only dependent state.

## 9. Risks, mitigations, and stop conditions

| Risk | Concrete consequence | Mitigation |
|---|---|---|
| Authority drift | A predecessor, external project, UI, model, or renderer is treated as current product authority. | Require exact source disposition, current authority validation, and product-boundary tests. |
| False completion | A synthetic URI, dry-run, unverified command, or model self-report is promoted as a real result. | Require actual files, hashes, independent validation, and artifact-class labels. |
| Over-broad automation | A model or agent gains tools, context, or authority beyond the current node. | Use JIT context, node-local tool grants, sandboxes, and explicit escalation. |
| Hidden mutation | Accepted meaning, source, program, or human preference changes without a versioned record. | Use immutable versions, typed commands, receipts, and selective invalidation. |

**Stop conditions**

- The behavior would create a second semantic or canonical state owner.
- A required source, right, authority, contract, runtime, evaluator, or human decision is unavailable or unverified.
- The implementation would treat migration evidence or an external project as current authority.
- The change would imply real output, production readiness, or certification beyond available evidence.

## 10. Planning and implementation handoff

This module is implementation-ready only after its FRs have one primary vertical Story owner, its Stories pass CBAR hardening, its candidate Tech Specs identify exact existing code and target paths, and Program Control issues a bounded Development Capsule. Until then, this module is a product-authority draft.

*This feature module belongs to the Conscious Activations Atomic Harness Pipeline PRD V1.1 source-first reconciliation package.*

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given current authority, valid inputs, and an eligible execution binding, when this behavior runs, then rendered outputs shall pass ffprobe, frame sampling, audio checks, transcript/caption checks and delivery-profile validation and the downstream consumer receives a contract-valid result.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given stale, ineligible, ambiguous, out-of-scope, or unverifiable inputs, when this behavior is requested, then no unauthorized side effect occurs and a typed blocker names the cause, owner, and next admissible action.
- **Evidence required:** runtime integration tests, version/fingerprint receipts, real renders, ffprobe/frame/audio/caption QA, and export manifests, linked to an immutable requirement receipt.

**Governing decisions:** D023, D027, D028, D029, D030, D035  
**Exact source references:** SRC-LEG-013, SRC-LEG-014, SRC-LEG-015, SRC-LEG-016, SRC-LEG-017, SRC-LEG-018, SRC-EXT-007, SRC-EXT-012, SRC-EXT-013, SRC-EXT-014


### FR-078 — Package final delivery artifacts

**Lifecycle:** `PRESERVED_AND_DEEPENED`  
**Normative requirement:** Export shall emit artifact hashes, codec/container profile, manifests, previews, logs and technical QA receipts.

**Trigger and preconditions:** When a validated run, planning action, or operator request requires `Package final delivery artifacts` within feature F13.

**Required output or state transition:** A versioned, inspectable result or governed record that satisfies this requirement and can be consumed by the declared downstream owner.

**Authority and invariants:**
- Adapters do not read complete doctrine or choose strategy.
- No silent runtime substitution.
- Actual output and process are verified.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given current authority, valid inputs, and an eligible execution binding, when this behavior runs, then export shall emit artifact hashes, codec/container profile, manifests, previews, logs and technical QA receipts and the downstream consumer receives a contract-valid result.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given stale, ineligible, ambiguous, out-of-scope, or unverifiable inputs, when this behavior is requested, then no unauthorized side effect occurs and a typed blocker names the cause, owner, and next admissible action.
- **Evidence required:** runtime integration tests, version/fingerprint receipts, real renders, ffprobe/frame/audio/caption QA, and export manifests, linked to an immutable requirement receipt.

**Governing decisions:** D023, D027, D028, D029, D030, D035  
**Exact source references:** SRC-LEG-013, SRC-LEG-014, SRC-LEG-015, SRC-LEG-016, SRC-LEG-017, SRC-LEG-018, SRC-EXT-007, SRC-EXT-012, SRC-EXT-013, SRC-EXT-014


## 7. Execution, model, tool, and human responsibilities

Deterministic services own mechanically decidable facts. Programmed Models or bounded Agent Programs may propose or compile behavior only within their evidence-backed claim and node-local tool grants. Independent evaluators inspect judgment dimensions. Humans own new meaning, consent, identity, unresolved taste, policy exceptions, promotion, and publication authority where assigned. The producing model or runtime cannot accept its own output.

When the feature uses a Hunter, Analyst, Composer, or Commander role, the role is an explicit workflow responsibility. It may be implemented by code, a small model, a larger model, or a human. The role name never hides the actual actor or expand its authority.

## 8. Validation and quality gates

Validation must prove both the intended result and the process that produced it. The minimum feature evidence includes runtime integration tests, version/fingerprint receipts, real renders, ffprobe/frame/audio/caption QA, and export manifests. Mechanical tests run before expensive model or visual evaluation. Judgment evaluators are calibrated to the exact category and context. Every denial names the cause, owner, and next admissible action. Every accepted mutation emits an immutable receipt and updates only dependent state.

## 9. Risks, mitigations, and stop conditions

| Risk | Concrete consequence | Mitigation |
|---|---|---|
| Authority drift | A predecessor, external project, UI, model, or renderer is treated as current product authority. | Require exact source disposition, current authority validation, and product-boundary tests. |
| False completion | A synthetic URI, dry-run, unverified command, or model self-report is promoted as a real result. | Require actual files, hashes, independent validation, and artifact-class labels. |
| Over-broad automation | A model or agent gains tools, context, or authority beyond the current node. | Use JIT context, node-local tool grants, sandboxes, and explicit escalation. |
| Hidden mutation | Accepted meaning, source, program, or human preference changes without a versioned record. | Use immutable versions, typed commands, receipts, and selective invalidation. |

**Stop conditions**

- The behavior would create a second semantic or canonical state owner.
- A required source, right, authority, contract, runtime, evaluator, or human decision is unavailable or unverified.
- The implementation would treat migration evidence or an external project as current authority.
- The change would imply real output, production readiness, or certification beyond available evidence.

## 10. Planning and implementation handoff

This module is implementation-ready only after its FRs have one primary vertical Story owner, its Stories pass CBAR hardening, its candidate Tech Specs identify exact existing code and target paths, and Program Control issues a bounded Development Capsule. Until then, this module is a product-authority draft.

*This feature module belongs to the Conscious Activations Atomic Harness Pipeline PRD V1.1 source-first reconciliation package.*

# F14 — Deferred Format 02 Historical Reconciliation

## 1. Product claim and user outcome

**User outcome:** Format 02 evidence is preserved without claiming an active runtime, Studio surface, or production path before the current Harness exists.

Protect valuable predecessor registries, schemas, tests, and embodiment research while enforcing the current deferral gate. This feature exists to convert doctrine and source evidence into behavior that can be implemented, tested, denied, replayed, and audited. It does not grant implementation, provider, model-training, publication, production, or certification authority by itself.

## 2. Product boundary and ownership

Program Control owns the deferral state. No runtime or Studio implementation owner is active.

The feature must preserve the current product topology. Builder supplies the immutable Atomic Harness; Pipeline executes its declared nodes; Interview Expression owns source expression preparation and approval; VAE owns visual production; Delegation owns cross-product envelopes; Studio projects state and emits typed operator commands; Program Control owns cross-product authority and release truth. External renderers and models are embodiments, not sources of meaning.

## 3. Canonical objects and state

The feature consumes current, versioned upstream records and emits typed outputs that remain linked to the active Harness, source package where applicable, Workflow Node, JIT Capsule, execution binding, evaluator, and receipt. Canonical records use stable serialization and immutable identities. A UI projection, model response, provider job, renderer workspace, or local cache cannot become accepted product state until its contract and authority gates pass.

Core invariants for this feature are:

- Format 02 remains inactive.
- Historical evidence is not current authority.
- Future specs are regenerated from a validated current Harness.

## 4. Brownfield and external capability treatment

The implementation begins from exact current and predecessor evidence. The table below identifies the most relevant source records. `REUSE` or `ADAPT` permits bounded implementation reuse after namespace, authority, license, dependency, and behavior review; it never imports historical product meaning automatically.

| Source | Disposition | Exact path or reference | Role |
|---|---|---|---|
| `SRC-AM-001` | `AMENDMENT_INPUT` | CONSCIOUS_ACTIVATIONS_STUDIO_ARCHITECTURE_AMENDMENT_V2_1(2).zip | Format 02 deferral, HumanResolutionEpisode, supervisory Studio, autonomy modes, timeline adoption, and Revision Compiler. |
| `SRC-CUR-006` | `REFERENCE` | 01_ATOMIC_HARNESS_BUILDER/src/cmf_builder/domain/format_profiles.py | Current edited-video, Format 02 and conversational profile identities. |
| `SRC-CUR-021` | `REFERENCE` | 02_VISUAL_ASSET_EDITOR/CURRENT_PROJECT_STATUS.md | Public VAE implementation/evidence status and Stage 5 gate. |
| `SRC-MIG-001` | `REFERENCE` | CMF_STUDIO_PREDECESSOR_MIGRATION_AUDIT_V1(1).md | Defines brownfield reuse/adapt/rewrite/archive treatment for the CMF Studio predecessor. |
| `SRC-EXT-018` | `REFERENCE_LICENSE_REVIEW` | github://remotion-dev/remotion | React/frame source-of-truth rendering, Player, batch rendering, and editor integration. |
| `SRC-EXT-019` | `REFERENCE` | github://heygen-com/hyperframes | Deterministic HTML/CSS/GSAP motion blocks, skills, registry, Studio, and Player. |
| `SRC-EXT-025` | `REFERENCE` | github://MangoLion/stretchystudio | Layered PSD rigging, mesh deformation, keyframe timeline, shape keys, and 2D animation embodiment. |

## 5. Workflow integration

Validated upstream state → feature behavior → typed output and receipt → downstream handoff → evaluation, invalidation, and replay.

Every handoff is typed. A downstream node begins only after the producer output passes the declared contract and evidence gates. Failures are attributed to source, knowledge, retrieval, Skill, recipe, Programmed Model, tool, runtime, product, evaluator, or human-policy layers before repair or escalation.

## 6. Functional Requirements

### FR-079 — Keep Format 02 outside the active implementation queue

**Lifecycle:** `AMENDED_V1_1`  
**Normative requirement:** The Pipeline shall record Format 02 as DEFERRED_AWAITING_CURRENT_ATOMIC_HARNESS and shall not implement, expose, benchmark, or claim an executable character-performance path until the current Builder emits and independent validation accepts the complete current Format 02 AtomicHarnessDefinition.

**Trigger and preconditions:** Planning, binding, Studio routing, or release evaluation encounters Format 02.

**Required output or state transition:** A typed deferred-scope record, blocked implementation status, historical-input inventory, and activation prerequisites.

**Authority and invariants:**
- No historical spec or prototype grants current authority.
- No Format 02 Studio surface is active.
- No runtime, benchmark, production, or certification claim is emitted.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given an attempt to add a Format 02 lane, when the current Harness is absent, then planning records the exact activation gate and excludes the lane from the active campaign.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given a predecessor golden-path fixture, when a component attempts to treat it as an executable current Harness, then authority validation fails.
- **Evidence required:** Scope-correction receipt, Program Control status, and absence checks for active bindings, routes, and release claims.

**Governing decisions:** D031, D051  
**Exact source references:** SRC-AM-001, SRC-CUR-006, SRC-CUR-021, SRC-MIG-001


### FR-080 — Preserve the 13 registry families as future reconciliation requirements

**Lifecycle:** `AMENDED_V1_1`  
**Normative requirement:** The historical character identity, pose, expression, gesture, gaze, props, animation primitives, state, scene relationships, camera/framing, transitions, sonic cues, and compatibility registries shall remain evidence inputs for future Harness reconciliation but shall not be instantiated as active Pipeline authority.

**Trigger and preconditions:** Format 02 historical material is inventoried or migrated.

**Required output or state transition:** A future-reconciliation registry inventory with source hashes, dispositions, gaps, and no active runtime status.

**Authority and invariants:**
- Registry evidence remains immutable.
- Current Harness authority must supersede historical assumptions.
- No automatic promotion from evidence to production registry.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given historical registry artifacts, when migration inventory runs, then all thirteen families are preserved with exact provenance and marked future-use only.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given an old registry item with a conflicting current category rule, when reconciliation is absent, then it cannot enter an active JIT Capsule or binding.
- **Evidence required:** Registry inventory, hash manifest, authority disposition, and conflict report.

**Governing decisions:** D031, D051

### FR-081 — Retain CharacterPerformanceProgram as a future renderer-neutral contract candidate

- No candidate schema is labeled current.
- Renderer-specific assumptions are not promoted.

- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given a request to generate a current program from the old schema alone, when authority checks run, then the request is denied.

**Governing decisions:** D031, D051

### FR-084 — Use predecessor Format 02 assets only as historical migration evidence

**Lifecycle:** `AMENDED_V1_1`

- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given a synthetic URI or old approval flag, when a release report is generated, then it is excluded from real-output and readiness evidence.
- **Evidence required:** Migration manifest, artifact classification, test isolation, and claim-ceiling validation.

**Governing decisions:** D031, D051  
**Exact source references:** SRC-MIG-001, SRC-AM-001

# F15 — Visual Asset Editor, Delegation, and GNM Boundary Integration

## 1. Product claim and user outcome

**User outcome:** The Pipeline requests visual ingredients through typed boundaries and consumes measured VAE results while VAE owns production methods such as SAM3, Lucida, layered providers, ComfyUI, and GNM.

Preserve product sovereignty from source-grounded demand through evaluated Asset Result and usage acknowledgement. This feature exists to convert doctrine and source evidence into behavior that can be implemented, tested, denied, replayed, and audited. It does not grant implementation, provider, model-training, publication, production, or certification authority by itself.

## 2. Product boundary and ownership

Pipeline owns demand/result orchestration; VAE owns visual production methods; Delegation owns cross-product lifecycle.

The feature must preserve the current product topology. Builder supplies the immutable Atomic Harness; Pipeline executes its declared nodes; Interview Expression owns source expression preparation and approval; VAE owns visual production; Delegation owns cross-product envelopes; Studio projects state and emits typed operator commands; Program Control owns cross-product authority and release truth. External renderers and models are embodiments, not sources of meaning.

## 3. Canonical objects and state

The feature consumes current, versioned upstream records and emits typed outputs that remain linked to the active Harness, source package where applicable, Workflow Node, JIT Capsule, execution binding, evaluator, and receipt. Canonical records use stable serialization and immutable identities. A UI projection, model response, provider job, renderer workspace, or local cache cannot become accepted product state until its contract and authority gates pass.

Core invariants for this feature are:

- Pipeline does not implement VAE providers.
- GNM supplies geometry, not human truth.
- Demand/result identity and evaluation gate continuation.

## 4. Brownfield and external capability treatment

## 6. Functional Requirements

### FR-085 — Emit immutable source-grounded Visual Asset Demands through Delegation

**Lifecycle:** `AMENDED_V1_1`  
**Normative requirement:** When a source-backed content job lacks or must repair a visual ingredient, the Pipeline shall emit an immutable Visual Asset Demand through Delegation containing the exact source lineage, semantic and composition role, asset family, geometry need, permitted variation, preservation locks, budget, deadline, and evaluation contract.

**Trigger and preconditions:** A Workflow Node proves that an accepted composition or edit requires an unavailable, incompatible, or failed visual ingredient.

**Required output or state transition:** A versioned Delegation request linked to the source package, Expression Moment or evidence object, Harness, node, and composition/timeline program.

**Authority and invariants:**
- Pipeline does not plan VAE production strategy.
- The demand cannot mutate source meaning.
- Source-derived identity/expression references remain attributable.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given a Carousel slide requiring a source-grounded portrait cutout, when the asset is unavailable, then the demand includes the exact keyframe/source-time reference and intended composition region.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given an agent that decides to generate a decorative image without an accepted role or demand, when admission runs, then Delegation is not invoked.
- **Evidence required:** Demand hash, lineage graph, authority check, budget reservation, and Delegation submission receipt.

**Governing decisions:** D004, D028, D030, D044, D050  
**Exact source references:** SRC-CUR-014, SRC-CUR-016, SRC-CUR-022, SRC-AM-002, SRC-INT-001


### FR-086 — Consume VAE Asset Results with image-conditioned geometry

**Lifecycle:** `AMENDED_V1_1`  
**Normative requirement:** The Pipeline shall consume accepted VAE Asset Results only after validating request/result identity, source and derivative lineage, asset-family scope, measured geometry, masks, gaze or motion, depth/layers, safe crops, negative-space regions, limitations, evaluation evidence, and downstream compatibility.

**Trigger and preconditions:** Delegation returns a candidate or accepted Asset Result.

**Required output or state transition:** A validated production-asset reference and geometry pack eligible for the requesting Composition or VideoEditProgram.

**Authority and invariants:**
- An asset result cannot silently change the demand.
- Limitations remain visible downstream.
- The producing model cannot self-approve.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given a returned portrait derivative, when validation passes, then the Pipeline can place it using measured face/subject BBOXes and safe crop data without rerunning the producer.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given a visually attractive asset with missing demand identity or evaluator evidence, when continuation is requested, then the Pipeline blocks the downstream node.
- **Evidence required:** Demand/result match report, geometry validation, evaluator receipts, artifact hashes, and acknowledgement/usage receipt.

**Governing decisions:** D004, D028, D030, D044, D050  
**Exact source references:** SRC-CUR-014, SRC-CUR-016, SRC-CUR-018, SRC-CUR-022


### FR-087 — Keep SAM3 execution inside the Visual Asset Editor

**Lifecycle:** `AMENDED_V1_1`  
**Normative requirement:** SAM3 segmentation and tracking shall be implemented, versioned, evaluated, and operated by the Visual Asset Editor behind its provider and capability interfaces; the Pipeline owns only demand, result, health, and receipt integration.

**Trigger and preconditions:** A VAE route requires concept-conditioned segmentation or tracking.

**Required output or state transition:** VAE-owned masks, tracks, geometry evidence, model/runtime identities, and Asset Result references.

**Authority and invariants:**
- No SAM3 worker is implemented inside Pipeline core.
- Pipeline does not claim VAE provider capability.
- Provider output remains independently evaluated.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given a VAE plan selecting SAM3, when the worker succeeds, then the Pipeline receives only the contract-defined result and evidence.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given a Pipeline node attempting to call SAM3 directly to bypass VAE planning, when ownership validation runs, then the action is denied.
- **Evidence required:** Product-boundary test, VAE capability receipt, Delegation result, and Pipeline consumer conformance.

**Governing decisions:** D004, D050  
**Exact source references:** SRC-CUR-013, SRC-CUR-015, SRC-CUR-016, SRC-MIG-001


### FR-088 — Keep Lucida matting evaluation inside the Visual Asset Editor

**Lifecycle:** `AMENDED_V1_1`  
**Normative requirement:** Lucida or any replacement matting provider may be evaluated and, if authorized, executed only within the VAE capability registry and production plan; the Pipeline shall not own provider selection or matting semantics.

**Trigger and preconditions:** The VAE determines that alpha refinement is required for an asset family and route.

**Required output or state transition:** VAE-owned matte artifacts, benchmark/evaluation evidence, limitations, and Asset Result bindings.

**Authority and invariants:**
- License and model evidence must be approved.
- Provider choice remains VAE-owned.
- Pipeline sees only typed result status and artifacts.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given an approved Lucida capability and a typography cutout demand, when VAE executes, then matte evidence is packaged with the result.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given an unreviewed model or license, when a production plan tries to bind it, then VAE blocks before execution and Pipeline receives a typed blocker.
- **Evidence required:** Capability registry state, benchmark report, license review, output hashes, and result receipt.

**Governing decisions:** D004, D050  
**Exact source references:** SRC-CUR-013, SRC-CUR-015, SRC-CUR-016, SRC-MIG-001


### FR-089 — Keep layered visual generation and GNM behind VAE capability routing

**Lifecycle:** `AMENDED_V1_1`  
**Normative requirement:** Layered image providers, ComfyUI workflows, and Google GNM facial-geometry references shall remain VAE-owned capabilities selected by the Visual Production Plan; they are not Pipeline, Interview Expression, or identity-authority components.

**Trigger and preconditions:** A Visual Asset Demand requires layer-separated generation, controlled facial geometry, expression reference, pose/gaze reference, or another specialist visual route.

**Required output or state transition:** VAE plan decisions, bounded provider artifacts, geometry/reference passes, evaluation, and Asset Result lineage.

**Authority and invariants:**
- GNM does not infer human identity or emotional truth.
- Real-person identity comes from approved source references and fitting evidence, not demographic sampling.
- Provider outputs cannot approve themselves.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given an approved source-backed Expression Moment and demand for a controlled head-pose reference, when VAE selects GNM, then the resulting mesh/render references preserve source identity lineage and are labeled geometric controls.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given a request to generate a real coach identity from GNM demographic labels, when validation runs, then the route is prohibited.
- **Evidence required:** VAE route receipt, source-reference binding, GNM/version identity, geometry outputs, fairness/limitation acknowledgement, and independent evaluation.

**Governing decisions:** D004, D050  
**Exact source references:** SRC-CUR-015, SRC-CUR-016, SRC-EXT-026, SRC-AM-002, SRC-MIG-001


### FR-090 — Validate Asset Results and downstream usage before continuation

**Lifecycle:** `AMENDED_V1_1`  
**Normative requirement:** The Pipeline shall resume composition only after the VAE result passes demand identity, authority, source lineage, geometry, evaluation, artifact integrity, supersession, and usage-acknowledgement checks.

**Trigger and preconditions:** A VAE result is proposed for use by a static, temporal, or animation derivative.

**Required output or state transition:** An accepted production asset binding, downstream usage record, invalidation dependencies, or typed rejection.

**Authority and invariants:**
- Result-ready is not completed until downstream acknowledgement where required.
- Rejected assets remain historical.
- Supersession invalidates only affected descendants.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given an evaluated result with complete geometry, when the requesting program acknowledges exact use, then the Pipeline resumes and records the consumption relationship.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given a superseded or revoked asset, when a cached composition attempts to use it, then eligibility fails and only affected descendants are invalidated.
- **Evidence required:** Validation report, usage acknowledgement, asset/version lineage, and selective invalidation receipt.

**Governing decisions:** D004, D028, D030, D044, D050  
**Exact source references:** SRC-CUR-014, SRC-CUR-018, SRC-CUR-019, SRC-CUR-022


## 7. Execution, model, tool, and human responsibilities

Deterministic services own mechanically decidable facts. Programmed Models or bounded Agent Programs may propose or compile behavior only within their evidence-backed claim and node-local tool grants. Independent evaluators inspect judgment dimensions. Humans own new meaning, consent, identity, unresolved taste, policy exceptions, promotion, and publication authority where assigned. The producing model or runtime cannot accept its own output.

When the feature uses a Hunter, Analyst, Composer, or Commander role, the role is an explicit workflow responsibility. It may be implemented by code, a small model, a larger model, or a human. The role name never hides the actual actor or expand its authority.

## 8. Validation and quality gates

Validation must prove both the intended result and the process that produced it. The minimum feature evidence includes Delegation conformance, demand/result lineage, VAE capability receipts, geometry validation, and downstream acknowledgement. Mechanical tests run before expensive model or visual evaluation. Judgment evaluators are calibrated to the exact category and context. Every denial names the cause, owner, and next admissible action. Every accepted mutation emits an immutable receipt and updates only dependent state.

## 9. Risks, mitigations, and stop conditions

| Risk | Concrete consequence | Mitigation |
|---|---|---|
| Authority drift | A predecessor, external project, UI, model, or renderer is treated as current product authority. | Require exact source disposition, current authority validation, and product-boundary tests. |
| False completion | A synthetic URI, dry-run, unverified command, or model self-report is promoted as a real result. | Require actual files, hashes, independent validation, and artifact-class labels. |
| Over-broad automation | A model or agent gains tools, context, or authority beyond the current node. | Use JIT context, node-local tool grants, sandboxes, and explicit escalation. |
| Hidden mutation | Accepted meaning, source, program, or human preference changes without a versioned record. | Use immutable versions, typed commands, receipts, and selective invalidation. |
| GNM identity misuse | Generic identity sampling or expression labels are treated as real-person identity or emotional truth. | Require source-backed fitting/references, VAE ownership, explicit geometric-control labels, and route prohibition tests. |

**Stop conditions**

- The behavior would create a second semantic or canonical state owner.
- A required source, right, authority, contract, runtime, evaluator, or human decision is unavailable or unverified.
- The implementation would treat migration evidence or an external project as current authority.
- The change would imply real output, production readiness, or certification beyond available evidence.

## 10. Planning and implementation handoff

This module is implementation-ready only after its FRs have one primary vertical Story owner, its Stories pass CBAR hardening, its candidate Tech Specs identify exact existing code and target paths, and Program Control issues a bounded Development Capsule. Until then, this module is a product-authority draft.

*This feature module belongs to the Conscious Activations Atomic Harness Pipeline PRD V1.1 source-first reconciliation package.*


---

# F16 — Independent Evaluation, Visual Syntax Reparse, Diagnosis, and Selective Repair

## 1. Product claim and user outcome

**User outcome:** Production output is mechanically verified, independently evaluated, attributed to the responsible layer, and locally repaired.

Separate deterministic facts from judgment, compare intended and observed composition/timing, and preserve already-valid work. This feature exists to convert doctrine and source evidence into behavior that can be implemented, tested, denied, replayed, and audited. It does not grant implementation, provider, model-training, publication, production, or certification authority by itself.

## 2. Product boundary and ownership

The owning product is the Atomic Harness Pipeline unless an FR explicitly assigns Interview Expression, VAE, Delegation, Studio, Program Control, or an external runtime.

The feature must preserve the current product topology. Builder supplies the immutable Atomic Harness; Pipeline executes its declared nodes; Interview Expression owns source expression preparation and approval; VAE owns visual production; Delegation owns cross-product envelopes; Studio projects state and emits typed operator commands; Program Control owns cross-product authority and release truth. External renderers and models are embodiments, not sources of meaning.

## 3. Canonical objects and state

The feature consumes current, versioned upstream records and emits typed outputs that remain linked to the active Harness, source package where applicable, Workflow Node, JIT Capsule, execution binding, evaluator, and receipt. Canonical records use stable serialization and immutable identities. A UI projection, model response, provider job, renderer workspace, or local cache cannot become accepted product state until its contract and authority gates pass.

Core invariants for this feature are:

- Producer cannot approve itself.
- Failure attribution distinguishes retrieval/model/tool/runtime/evaluator.
- Repair changes only permitted units.

## 4. Brownfield and external capability treatment

The implementation begins from exact current and predecessor evidence. The table below identifies the most relevant source records. `REUSE` or `ADAPT` permits bounded implementation reuse after namespace, authority, license, dependency, and behavior review; it never imports historical product meaning automatically.

| Source | Disposition | Exact path or reference | Role |
|---|---|---|---|
| `SRC-CUR-018` | `REFERENCE` | 02_VISUAL_ASSET_EDITOR/prd/05-features/F14-visual-evaluation-profiles.md | Independent visual evaluation profiles. |
| `SRC-CUR-019` | `REFERENCE` | 02_VISUAL_ASSET_EDITOR/prd/05-features/F15-repair-invalidation-reruns.md | Typed visual repair and bounded reruns. |
| `SRC-LEG-019` | `FORK` | src/ccp_studio/contracts/render_qa.py | Technical QA contracts and receipts. |
| `SRC-LEG-020` | `FORK_ADAPT` | src/ccp_studio/services/render_qa_service.py | Add Visual Syntax reparse and separate technical vs creative evaluation. |
| `SRC-LEG-021` | `FORK_ACTIVATE` | src/ccp_studio/services/ffprobe_validation_service.py | Technical media validation. |
| `SRC-LEG-022` | `FORK_ACTIVATE` | src/ccp_studio/services/frame_sampling_service.py | Deterministic frame sampling for review/evaluation. |
| `SRC-LEG-023` | `FORK_ACTIVATE` | src/ccp_studio/services/audio_level_analysis_service.py | Audio-level evidence. |

## 5. Workflow integration

Validated upstream state → feature behavior → typed output and receipt → downstream handoff → evaluation, invalidation, and replay.

Every handoff is typed. A downstream node begins only after the producer output passes the declared contract and evidence gates. Failures are attributed to source, knowledge, retrieval, Skill, recipe, Programmed Model, tool, runtime, product, evaluator, or human-policy layers before repair or escalation.

## 6. Functional Requirements

### FR-091 — Verify mechanically decidable conditions

**Lifecycle:** `PRESERVED_AND_DEEPENED`  
**Normative requirement:** Contracts, geometry, text fit, timing, source lineage, tool use, export and execution-envelope conditions shall use deterministic verification.

**Trigger and preconditions:** When a validated run, planning action, or operator request requires `Verify mechanically decidable conditions` within feature F16.

**Required output or state transition:** A versioned, inspectable result or governed record that satisfies this requirement and can be consumed by the declared downstream owner.

**Authority and invariants:**
- Producer cannot approve itself.
- Failure attribution distinguishes retrieval/model/tool/runtime/evaluator.
- Repair changes only permitted units.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given current authority, valid inputs, and an eligible execution binding, when this behavior runs, then contracts, geometry, text fit, timing, source lineage, tool use, export and execution-envelope conditions shall use deterministic verification and the downstream consumer receives a contract-valid result.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given stale, ineligible, ambiguous, out-of-scope, or unverifiable inputs, when this behavior is requested, then no unauthorized side effect occurs and a typed blocker names the cause, owner, and next admissible action.
- **Evidence required:** deterministic validators, evaluator calibration, rendered reparse, diagnosis accuracy, selective rerun, and escalation, linked to an immutable requirement receipt.

**Governing decisions:** D023, D024, D025, D035, D036, D040  
**Exact source references:** SRC-CUR-018, SRC-CUR-019, SRC-LEG-019, SRC-LEG-020, SRC-LEG-021, SRC-LEG-022, SRC-LEG-023

# F17 — Evidence, Human Resolution, Steering Intelligence, and Programmed Model Learning Flywheel

## 1. Product claim and user outcome

**User outcome:** Every production and human-resolution episode strengthens explicit knowledge and offline learned capability evidence without live uncontrolled mutation.

Capture exact before/after state, attribute causes, build rights-aware datasets, promote recipes and models through evidence, and retain rollback. This feature exists to convert doctrine and source evidence into behavior that can be implemented, tested, denied, replayed, and audited. It does not grant implementation, provider, model-training, publication, production, or certification authority by itself.

## 2. Product boundary and ownership

The owning product is the Atomic Harness Pipeline unless an FR explicitly assigns Interview Expression, VAE, Delegation, Studio, Program Control, or an external runtime.

The feature must preserve the current product topology. Builder supplies the immutable Atomic Harness; Pipeline executes its declared nodes; Interview Expression owns source expression preparation and approval; VAE owns visual production; Delegation owns cross-product envelopes; Studio projects state and emits typed operator commands; Program Control owns cross-product authority and release truth. External renderers and models are embodiments, not sources of meaning.

## 3. Canonical objects and state

The feature consumes current, versioned upstream records and emits typed outputs that remain linked to the active Harness, source package where applicable, Workflow Node, JIT Capsule, execution binding, evaluator, and receipt. Canonical records use stable serialization and immutable identities. A UI projection, model response, provider job, renderer workspace, or local cache cannot become accepted product state until its contract and authority gates pass.

Core invariants for this feature are:

- Capture/indexing is automatic; promotion is not.
- Human preference is scoped.
- Rights and consent govern learning.

## 4. Brownfield and external capability treatment

The implementation begins from exact current and predecessor evidence. The table below identifies the most relevant source records. `REUSE` or `ADAPT` permits bounded implementation reuse after namespace, authority, license, dependency, and behavior review; it never imports historical product meaning automatically.

| Source | Disposition | Exact path or reference | Role |
|---|---|---|---|
| `SRC-CUR-020` | `REFERENCE` | 02_VISUAL_ASSET_EDITOR/prd/05-features/F17-steering-intelligence-cmf-okf-retrieval.md | CMF-OKF, Steering Recipes, hybrid retrieval and Minimum Complete Context. |
| `SRC-AM-001` | `AMENDMENT_INPUT` | CONSCIOUS_ACTIVATIONS_STUDIO_ARCHITECTURE_AMENDMENT_V2_1(2).zip | Format 02 deferral, HumanResolutionEpisode, supervisory Studio, autonomy modes, timeline adoption, and Revision Compiler. |
| `SRC-AM-002` | `AMENDMENT_INPUT` | PA_AM_001_SEVEN_DAY_PARALLEL_PRODUCTION_ACTIVATION_V1_1(2).zip | Parallel Pipeline, temporal, static, VAE, Interview Expression, GNM, and retrieval/model-program activation lanes. |
| `SRC-EXT-001` | `REFERENCE` | file:///mnt/data/Agentic Prompt Enhancer for Image Generation and.pdf | Trainable small prompt enhancers; router–rewriter–composer and downstream-output reward. |
| `SRC-EXT-005` | `REFERENCE` | https://huggingface.co/nvidia/Nemotron-3-Embed-1B-BF16 | Text/code dense retrieval candidate after deterministic eligibility filtering. |

## 5. Workflow integration

Validated upstream state → feature behavior → typed output and receipt → downstream handoff → evaluation, invalidation, and replay.

Every handoff is typed. A downstream node begins only after the producer output passes the declared contract and evidence gates. Failures are attributed to source, knowledge, retrieval, Skill, recipe, Programmed Model, tool, runtime, product, evaluator, or human-policy layers before repair or escalation.

## 6. Functional Requirements

### FR-097 — Persist complete production and human-resolution episodes

**Lifecycle:** `AMENDED_V1_1`  
**Normative requirement:** Each accepted, rejected, repaired, escalated, and human-resolved production episode shall link the source package, Harness, run state, JIT Capsule, candidates, exact tool operations, renders, evaluations, decision authority, result, and downstream outcome.

**Trigger and preconditions:** A node, candidate portfolio, operator action, or campaign reaches a decision or terminal state.

**Required output or state transition:** Immutable ProductionEpisode and, where human authority acted, HumanResolutionEpisode records.

**Authority and invariants:**
- UI actions cannot disappear as anonymous state.
- Human scope and rationale remain explicit.
- No episode mutates live models or canonical doctrine.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given an operator moves a cut and accepts the preview, when the action commits, then the episode records before/after program state, exact tool command, affected nodes, evaluation, and acceptance scope.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given a manual change with no attributable authority or before-state identity, when persistence is requested, then the change cannot become accepted state.
- **Evidence required:** Episode hash, before/after references, tool/process receipts, human authority, and result lineage.

**Governing decisions:** D017, D024, D025, D026, D047  
**Exact source references:** SRC-CUR-020, SRC-AM-001, SRC-AM-002


### FR-098 — Attribute learning opportunities to the responsible layer

**Lifecycle:** `AMENDED_V1_1`  
**Normative requirement:** The system shall diagnose whether an episode indicates a source, knowledge, retrieval, context, Skill, Steering Recipe, Programmed Model, tool, runtime, VAE, evaluator, or human-policy opportunity before it enters any learning queue.

**Trigger and preconditions:** A production or human-resolution episode is closed.

**Required output or state transition:** A typed attribution record, candidate programming-material dispositions, and excluded interpretations.

**Authority and invariants:**
- Visible symptoms are not automatically assigned to the model.
- Attribution can remain uncertain or multi-causal.
- Promotion requires later evidence.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given a bad crop caused by a wrong geometry measurement, when diagnosis runs, then the episode is attributed to measurement/runtime rather than used to teach a taste model.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given a single operator rejection with no reason, when attribution is ambiguous, then the system stores it as scoped preference evidence but does not promote a universal recipe.
- **Evidence required:** Diagnosis report, responsible-layer confidence, excluded alternatives, and human review where required.

**Governing decisions:** D017, D024, D025, D026, D047  
**Exact source references:** SRC-CUR-020, SRC-AM-001, SRC-EXT-001, SRC-EXT-005


### FR-099 — Compile rights-aware versioned programming-material corpora

**Lifecycle:** `AMENDED_V1_1`  
**Normative requirement:** Supervised demonstrations, preference pairs, hard negatives, repair trajectories, retrieval-obedience cases, and revision-program examples shall be built offline from eligible episodes with exact rights, consent, provenance, scope, splits, hashes, and invalidation.

**Trigger and preconditions:** A model or evaluator team requests a dataset build for a bounded capability claim.

**Required output or state transition:** Versioned corpus manifest, training/validation/test partitions, exclusions, rights/consent scope, and source episode references.

**Authority and invariants:**
- Real-human source rights govern downstream training.
- Protected test data is isolated.
- No live-production mutation occurs.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given approved video-revision episodes, when a corpus is built, then source rights and identity scope are checked and the test split remains unavailable to the producer.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given an episode whose consent does not permit model training, when dataset selection runs, then it is excluded while remaining available for allowed operational audit if permitted.
- **Evidence required:** Dataset manifest, consent/rights report, split hashes, deduplication, leakage tests, and build receipt.

**Governing decisions:** D017, D024, D025, D026, D047  
**Exact source references:** SRC-CUR-020, SRC-AM-001


### FR-100 — Capture human preferences and corrections with explicit scope

**Lifecycle:** `AMENDED_V1_1`  
**Normative requirement:** Every operator approval, rejection, candidate selection, natural-language revision, direct manipulation, tool override, taste explanation, and publication decision shall produce a HumanResolutionEpisode whose applicability scope is explicit and nonuniversal by default.

**Trigger and preconditions:** A human takes an authorized action in any Studio surface or review queue.

**Required output or state transition:** A HumanResolutionEpisode with request, before/after state, operations, reasons, authority, learning scope, and candidate dispositions.

**Authority and invariants:**
- One decision never silently becomes universal doctrine.
- Direct UI manipulation and text requests produce equivalent evidence quality.
- Human identity is never synthesized on replay.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given a Carousel slide reorder, when the operator commits it, then the exact order change and stated reason are recorded with category/profile scope.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given an operator drag event without a resolved project/run/authority identity, when commit is attempted, then the UI must request resolution rather than writing anonymous state.
- **Evidence required:** Episode record, authority scope, exact changes, tool program, evaluation, and acceptance.

**Governing decisions:** D017, D024, D025, D026, D047  
**Exact source references:** SRC-AM-001, SRC-AM-002


### FR-101 — Promote Steering Recipes only through repeated evidence

**Lifecycle:** `AMENDED_V1_1`  
**Normative requirement:** Repeated successful, scoped interventions may advance a Steering Recipe through proposed, experimental, validated, shadow, limited-production, production, deprecated, and retired states with control comparisons, regression cases, human authority, and rollback.

**Trigger and preconditions:** Episode analysis identifies a recurring condition/intervention pattern.

**Required output or state transition:** A versioned Steering Recipe proposal or lifecycle transition with applicability, preserved properties, evidence, controls, failures, and rollback.

**Authority and invariants:**
- A raw winning prompt is not a recipe.
- A single success cannot change defaults.
- Contradictory and failed evidence remains linked.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given ten comparable hierarchy repairs and controls showing consistent improvement, when promotion is reviewed, then the recipe may enter shadow with exact scope and rollback.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given one visually appealing result and no control or failure cases, when promotion is requested, then the recipe remains proposed.
- **Evidence required:** Recipe evidence ledger, control comparison, regression suite, human promotion receipt, and rollback package.

**Governing decisions:** D017, D024, D025, D026, D047  
**Exact source references:** SRC-CUR-020, SRC-AM-001


### FR-102 — Prohibit uncontrolled online mutation while enabling automatic evidence capture

**Lifecycle:** `AMENDED_V1_1`  
**Normative requirement:** Production may automatically append immutable episodes, retrieval indexes, and programming-material eligibility records, but it shall not rewrite model weights, canonical Skills, Steering Recipes, authority rules, or production defaults without an offline evaluated release and human authorization.

**Trigger and preconditions:** A production episode or human correction completes.

**Required output or state transition:** Automatic evidence/index updates and, separately, an offline promotion candidate if eligible.

**Authority and invariants:**
- Capture is automatic; promotion is not.
- Historical evidence remains immutable.
- Release rollback is always possible.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given an accepted correction, when the episode closes, then retrieval can find it immediately while the production model remains unchanged.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given a service attempting to update an adapter checkpoint directly from a live click stream, when policy enforcement runs, then the mutation is blocked and incident evidence is recorded.
- **Evidence required:** Mutation-denial tests, index update receipt, model artifact immutability checks, and promotion workflow.

**Governing decisions:** D017, D024, D025, D026, D047  
**Exact source references:** SRC-CUR-020, SRC-AM-001


## 7. Execution, model, tool, and human responsibilities

Deterministic services own mechanically decidable facts. Programmed Models or bounded Agent Programs may propose or compile behavior only within their evidence-backed claim and node-local tool grants. Independent evaluators inspect judgment dimensions. Humans own new meaning, consent, identity, unresolved taste, policy exceptions, promotion, and publication authority where assigned. The producing model or runtime cannot accept its own output.

When the feature uses a Hunter, Analyst, Composer, or Commander role, the role is an explicit workflow responsibility. It may be implemented by code, a small model, a larger model, or a human. The role name never hides the actual actor or expand its authority.

## 8. Validation and quality gates

Validation must prove both the intended result and the process that produced it. The minimum feature evidence includes episode completeness, attribution, dataset lineage, retrieval indexing, shadow replay, recipe/model promotion, and mutation-denial. Mechanical tests run before expensive model or visual evaluation. Judgment evaluators are calibrated to the exact category and context. Every denial names the cause, owner, and next admissible action. Every accepted mutation emits an immutable receipt and updates only dependent state.

## 9. Risks, mitigations, and stop conditions

| Risk | Concrete consequence | Mitigation |
|---|---|---|
| Authority drift | A predecessor, external project, UI, model, or renderer is treated as current product authority. | Require exact source disposition, current authority validation, and product-boundary tests. |
| False completion | A synthetic URI, dry-run, unverified command, or model self-report is promoted as a real result. | Require actual files, hashes, independent validation, and artifact-class labels. |
| Over-broad automation | A model or agent gains tools, context, or authority beyond the current node. | Use JIT context, node-local tool grants, sandboxes, and explicit escalation. |
| Hidden mutation | Accepted meaning, source, program, or human preference changes without a versioned record. | Use immutable versions, typed commands, receipts, and selective invalidation. |

**Stop conditions**

- The behavior would create a second semantic or canonical state owner.
- A required source, right, authority, contract, runtime, evaluator, or human decision is unavailable or unverified.
- The implementation would treat migration evidence or an external project as current authority.
- The change would imply real output, production readiness, or certification beyond available evidence.

## 10. Planning and implementation handoff

This module is implementation-ready only after its FRs have one primary vertical Story owner, its Stories pass CBAR hardening, its candidate Tech Specs identify exact existing code and target paths, and Program Control issues a bounded Development Capsule. Until then, this module is a product-authority draft.

*This feature module belongs to the Conscious Activations Atomic Harness Pipeline PRD V1.1 source-first reconciliation package.*


---

# F18 — Execution Fingerprints, Sandbox, Continuous Assurance, and Incident Containment

## 1. Product claim and user outcome

**User outcome:** The system proves what executed and contains regressions without blanket recertification.

Record authorized and resolved execution stacks, enforce least-authority sandboxes, monitor signals, and restore known-good implementations. This feature exists to convert doctrine and source evidence into behavior that can be implemented, tested, denied, replayed, and audited. It does not grant implementation, provider, model-training, publication, production, or certification authority by itself.

## 2. Product boundary and ownership

The owning product is the Atomic Harness Pipeline unless an FR explicitly assigns Interview Expression, VAE, Delegation, Studio, Program Control, or an external runtime.

The feature must preserve the current product topology. Builder supplies the immutable Atomic Harness; Pipeline executes its declared nodes; Interview Expression owns source expression preparation and approval; VAE owns visual production; Delegation owns cross-product envelopes; Studio projects state and emits typed operator commands; Program Control owns cross-product authority and release truth. External renderers and models are embodiments, not sources of meaning.

## 3. Canonical objects and state

The feature consumes current, versioned upstream records and emits typed outputs that remain linked to the active Harness, source package where applicable, Workflow Node, JIT Capsule, execution binding, evaluator, and receipt. Canonical records use stable serialization and immutable identities. A UI projection, model response, provider job, renderer workspace, or local cache cannot become accepted product state until its contract and authority gates pass.

Core invariants for this feature are:

- Every side effect is observable.
- Material changes trigger focused regression.
- Incidents quarantine only affected claims.

## 4. Brownfield and external capability treatment

The implementation begins from exact current and predecessor evidence. The table below identifies the most relevant source records. `REUSE` or `ADAPT` permits bounded implementation reuse after namespace, authority, license, dependency, and behavior review; it never imports historical product meaning automatically.

| Source | Disposition | Exact path or reference | Role |
|---|---|---|---|
| `SRC-CUR-010` | `REFERENCE` | 01_ATOMIC_HARNESS_BUILDER/src/cmf_builder/workflow/actor_explicit_contracts.py | Execution-free Workflow Node, edge, authority and validation contracts. |
| `SRC-EXT-001` | `REFERENCE` | file:///mnt/data/Agentic Prompt Enhancer for Image Generation and.pdf | Trainable small prompt enhancers; router–rewriter–composer and downstream-output reward. |

## 5. Workflow integration

Validated upstream state → feature behavior → typed output and receipt → downstream handoff → evaluation, invalidation, and replay.

Every handoff is typed. A downstream node begins only after the producer output passes the declared contract and evidence gates. Failures are attributed to source, knowledge, retrieval, Skill, recipe, Programmed Model, tool, runtime, product, evaluator, or human-policy layers before repair or escalation.

## 6. Functional Requirements

### FR-103 — Emit composite execution-stack fingerprints

**Lifecycle:** `PRESERVED_AND_DEEPENED`  
**Normative requirement:** Every node attempt shall record the authorized and resolved model, context, tools, retrieval indexes, runtime, precision, hardware and evaluator identities.

**Trigger and preconditions:** When a validated run, planning action, or operator request requires `Emit composite execution-stack fingerprints` within feature F18.

**Required output or state transition:** A versioned, inspectable result or governed record that satisfies this requirement and can be consumed by the declared downstream owner.

**Authority and invariants:**
- Every side effect is observable.
- Material changes trigger focused regression.
- Incidents quarantine only affected claims.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given current authority, valid inputs, and an eligible execution binding, when this behavior runs, then every node attempt shall record the authorized and resolved model, context, tools, retrieval indexes, runtime, precision, hardware and evaluator identities and the downstream consumer receives a contract-valid result.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given stale, ineligible, ambiguous, out-of-scope, or unverifiable inputs, when this behavior is requested, then no unauthorized side effect occurs and a typed blocker names the cause, owner, and next admissible action.
- **Evidence required:** fingerprints, sandbox denials, process receipts, canary/drift metrics, containment and restore tests, linked to an immutable requirement receipt.

**Governing decisions:** D032, D033, D034, D037, D038  
**Exact source references:** SRC-CUR-010, SRC-EXT-001

# F19 — Conscious Activations Studio Control Tower and Category Workbenches

## 1. Product claim and user outcome

**User outcome:** Operators inspect source-to-batch production, approve genuine human decisions, request corrections, and replay evidence without becoming full-time editors.

Expose one shared supervisory shell with category-native modules, canonical-program projections, autonomy modes, health, evidence, and typed commands. This feature exists to convert doctrine and source evidence into behavior that can be implemented, tested, denied, replayed, and audited. It does not grant implementation, provider, model-training, publication, production, or certification authority by itself.

## 2. Product boundary and ownership

The owning product is the Atomic Harness Pipeline unless an FR explicitly assigns Interview Expression, VAE, Delegation, Studio, Program Control, or an external runtime.

The feature must preserve the current product topology. Builder supplies the immutable Atomic Harness; Pipeline executes its declared nodes; Interview Expression owns source expression preparation and approval; VAE owns visual production; Delegation owns cross-product envelopes; Studio projects state and emits typed operator commands; Program Control owns cross-product authority and release truth. External renderers and models are embodiments, not sources of meaning.

## 3. Canonical objects and state

The feature consumes current, versioned upstream records and emits typed outputs that remain linked to the active Harness, source package where applicable, Workflow Node, JIT Capsule, execution binding, evaluator, and receipt. Canonical records use stable serialization and immutable identities. A UI projection, model response, provider job, renderer workspace, or local cache cannot become accepted product state until its contract and authority gates pass.

Core invariants for this feature are:

- Studio read models are nonauthoritative.
- Direct manipulation uses typed command paths.
- Only assigned human authority receives actionable gates.

## 4. Brownfield and external capability treatment
