Failures are attributed to source, knowledge, retrieval, Skill, recipe, Programmed Model, tool, runtime, product, evaluator, or human-policy layers before repair or escalation.

## 6. Functional Requirements

### FR-109 — Expose source-to-batch run and graph projections

**Lifecycle:** `AMENDED_V1_1`  
**Normative requirement:** The Studio Control Tower shall show the Canonical Interview Source Package, content-batch jobs, Harnesses, phases, Workflow Nodes, bounded roles, owners, status, blockers, costs, artifacts, source-time lineage, and exact execution evidence.

**Trigger and preconditions:** An operator opens a project, source package, campaign, or run.

**Required output or state transition:** Live read models for source, batch, run graph, artifacts, evidence, human gates, and next admissible actions.

**Authority and invariants:**
- Read models do not become authority stores.
- Synthetic/dry-run/real artifact classes are unmistakable.
- Role labels do not hide actual execution actors.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given one interview producing a short, Carousel, and SuperVisual, when the batch board opens, then the operator can trace every output to the same source package and exact source spans.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given a UI fixture or stale projection that cannot prove its source state, when displayed, then it is labeled nonauthoritative and cannot drive a command.
- **Evidence required:** Read-model consistency tests, realtime event mapping, source-lineage drill-down, and projection freshness receipts.

**Governing decisions:** D005, D024, D031, D038, D046, D048, D052  
**Exact source references:** SRC-AM-001, SRC-AM-002, SRC-INT-001, SRC-MIG-001


### FR-110 — Provide category-native supervisory previews over canonical programs

**Lifecycle:** `AMENDED_V1_1`  
**Normative requirement:** Static, video, interview, VAE, and knowledge/model Studio modules shall display the current canonical programs, source evidence, assets, candidates, evaluations, repairs, and allowed human actions without owning hidden production state.

**Trigger and preconditions:** A run reaches a reviewable state or an operator enters a category-native Studio.

**Required output or state transition:** Interactive projections of Composition IR, VideoEditProgram, source transcript/time map, VAE demands/results, and model/retrieval evidence.

**Authority and invariants:**
- UI state round-trips into typed commands.
- Reopening reconstructs from canonical records.
- Direct manipulation cannot bypass validation.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given a video cut moved by drag, when committed, then the Studio emits the same typed ChangeRequestProgram as an equivalent natural-language request.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given a timeline edit stored only in browser memory, when the page reloads, then it is not accepted and the canonical timeline remains unchanged.
- **Evidence required:** Round-trip tests, command receipts, reload/replay tests, and UI/canonical-state consistency.

**Governing decisions:** D005, D024, D031, D048, D049  
**Exact source references:** SRC-AM-001, SRC-MIG-001, SRC-EXT-021, SRC-EXT-022


### FR-111 — Apply Harness autonomy modes and explicit human gates

**Lifecycle:** `AMENDED_V1_1`  
**Normative requirement:** Each campaign shall operate in AUTOPILOT, REVIEW_BEFORE_SHIP, CHECKPOINTED, or SHADOW mode, pausing only at declared human authority nodes, genuine exceptions, budget or policy changes, or unresolved taste boundaries.

**Trigger and preconditions:** A campaign is launched or a node encounters a human-owned condition.

**Required output or state transition:** An autonomy-policy binding, human-gate records, exception package, and resume decision.

**Authority and invariants:**
- Mature Harnesses target exception-only supervision.
- Humans are not asked to approve deterministic facts.
- No publication occurs beyond the mode’s authority.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given REVIEW_BEFORE_SHIP mode, when all production nodes pass, then one final acceptance is requested without intermediate pauses unless a genuine exception occurred.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given SHADOW mode, when all outputs pass evaluation, then publication remains prohibited.
- **Evidence required:** Autonomy binding, pause/resume logs, authority tests, and publication-denial receipt.

**Governing decisions:** D005, D024, D048  
**Exact source references:** SRC-AM-001, SRC-AM-002


### FR-112 — Inspect retrieval, Skills, recipes, Programmed Models, and exclusions

**Lifecycle:** `AMENDED_V1_1`  
**Normative requirement:** Operators shall be able to inspect the JIT Capsule, retrieved Skills and Steering Recipes, authority filters, exclusions, contradictory evidence, model claim envelope, benchmark evidence, limitations, fallbacks, and the reason each item influenced the current decision.

**Trigger and preconditions:** A learned, retrieval-backed, or taste-bearing node is reviewed.

**Required output or state transition:** A human-readable evidence view linked to exact retrieval and model receipts.

**Authority and invariants:**
- Similarity never appears as authority.
- Protected evaluator internals remain hidden.
- Unavailable context is disclosed.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given a static strategy proposal, when inspected, then the operator sees the selected Skill, two eligible recipes, one relevant negative precedent, and the exact exclusions.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given a semantically similar but wrong-category recipe, when the operator inspects retrieval, then it appears only in the exclusion evidence and not the active JIT Capsule.
- **Evidence required:** Retrieval receipt, claim manifest, benchmark links, and UI evidence tests.

**Governing decisions:** D005, D024, D048  
**Exact source references:** SRC-CUR-020, SRC-EXT-027, SRC-EXT-028, SRC-AM-002


### FR-113 — Expose runtime, provider, worker, and budget health

**Lifecycle:** `AMENDED_V1_1`  
**Normative requirement:** The Studio shall expose preflight, compatibility, health, queue, lease, resource, cost, and failure evidence for Skia, PRETEXT, FFmpeg, Remotion, HyperFrames, VAE providers, GNM, workers, and other bound embodiments without treating their presence as production certification.

**Trigger and preconditions:** An operator inspects a binding, campaign, active worker, blocker, or incident.

**Required output or state transition:** Capability and worker health projections, budget usage, exact blocker cause, owner, and next admissible action.

**Authority and invariants:**
- Health does not imply quality certification.
- Credentials and secrets are never exposed.
- Unavailable capabilities cannot be silently emulated.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given a failed Remotion worker preflight, when inspected, then the Studio shows the exact dependency/version failure and blocks only the affected nodes.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given a fake provider result or synthetic URI, when health/result views load, then the artifact is clearly nonproduction and cannot satisfy completion.
- **Evidence required:** Health receipts, worker heartbeats, budget ledger, blocker records, and security tests.

**Governing decisions:** D005, D024, D038, D050  
**Exact source references:** SRC-AM-002, SRC-MIG-001, SRC-EXT-018, SRC-EXT-019, SRC-EXT-026


### FR-114 — Export source-to-ship audit and replay packages

**Lifecycle:** `AMENDED_V1_1`  
**Normative requirement:** A completed campaign shall export the source package manifest, content-batch plan, Harnesses and bindings, JIT Capsules, typed programs, HumanResolutionEpisodes, artifacts, evaluations, execution fingerprints, logs, publication evidence, and replay instructions needed to reconstruct the accepted result.

**Trigger and preconditions:** A campaign reaches accepted, rejected, canceled, shadow-complete, or published terminal state.

**Required output or state transition:** A portable audit/replay bundle with exact hashes and claim boundaries.

**Authority and invariants:**
- No secrets or absolute machine paths.
- Historical human decisions are replayed as recorded rather than regenerated.
- External missing dependencies are declared.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given a published short and Carousel, when the audit package is opened elsewhere, then the source lineage and all accepted decisions can be verified even if rendering dependencies are unavailable.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given an artifact with no source or execution fingerprint, when export runs, then the bundle fails completeness validation.
- **Evidence required:** Portable bundle validation, hash manifest, secret/path scan, and clean-room replay report.

**Governing decisions:** D005, D024, D038, D044, D047  
**Exact source references:** SRC-AM-001, SRC-AM-002, SRC-MIG-001


## 7. Execution, model, tool, and human responsibilities

Deterministic services own mechanically decidable facts. Programmed Models or bounded Agent Programs may propose or compile behavior only within their evidence-backed claim and node-local tool grants. Independent evaluators inspect judgment dimensions. Humans own new meaning, consent, identity, unresolved taste, policy exceptions, promotion, and publication authority where assigned. The producing model or runtime cannot accept its own output.

When the feature uses a Hunter, Analyst, Composer, or Commander role, the role is an explicit workflow responsibility. It may be implemented by code, a small model, a larger model, or a human. The role name never hides the actual actor or expand its authority.

## 8. Validation and quality gates

Validation must prove both the intended result and the process that produced it. The minimum feature evidence includes read-model consistency, UI round-trip, autonomy/gate tests, role permissions, health projections, and audit exports. Mechanical tests run before expensive model or visual evaluation. Judgment evaluators are calibrated to the exact category and context. Every denial names the cause, owner, and next admissible action. Every accepted mutation emits an immutable receipt and updates only dependent state.

## 9. Risks, mitigations, and stop conditions

| Risk | Concrete consequence | Mitigation |
|---|---|---|
| Authority drift | A predecessor, external project, UI, model, or renderer is treated as current product authority. | Require exact source disposition, current authority validation, and product-boundary tests. |
| False completion | A synthetic URI, dry-run, unverified command, or model self-report is promoted as a real result. | Require actual files, hashes, independent validation, and artifact-class labels. |
| Over-broad automation | A model or agent gains tools, context, or authority beyond the current node. | Use JIT context, node-local tool grants, sandboxes, and explicit escalation. |
| Hidden mutation | Accepted meaning, source, program, or human preference changes without a versioned record. | Use immutable versions, typed commands, receipts, and selective invalidation. |

**Stop conditions**

- The behavior would create a second semantic or canonical state owner.
- A required source, right, authority, contract, runtime, evaluator, or human decision is unavailable or unverified.
- The implementation would treat migration evidence or an external project as current authority.
- The change would imply real output, production readiness, or certification beyond available evidence.

## 10. Planning and implementation handoff

This module is implementation-ready only after its FRs have one primary vertical Story owner, its Stories pass CBAR hardening, its candidate Tech Specs identify exact existing code and target paths, and Program Control issues a bounded Development Capsule. Until then, this module is a product-authority draft.

*This feature module belongs to the Conscious Activations Atomic Harness Pipeline PRD V1.1 source-first reconciliation package.*

# F20 — Source-First Release 1, Expansion, and Implementation Readiness

## 1. Product claim and user outcome

**User outcome:** The product proves one real interview-to-content-batch slice and expands only through evidence-backed boundaries.

Replace the static-only first slice with a real source-led short plus static derivative, human correction, evaluation, replay, and truthful claim states. This feature exists to convert doctrine and source evidence into behavior that can be implemented, tested, denied, replayed, and audited. It does not grant implementation, provider, model-training, publication, production, or certification authority by itself.

## 2. Product boundary and ownership

The owning product is the Atomic Harness Pipeline unless an FR explicitly assigns Interview Expression, VAE, Delegation, Studio, Program Control, or an external runtime.

The feature must preserve the current product topology. Builder supplies the immutable Atomic Harness; Pipeline executes its declared nodes; Interview Expression owns source expression preparation and approval; VAE owns visual production; Delegation owns cross-product envelopes; Studio projects state and emits typed operator commands; Program Control owns cross-product authority and release truth. External renderers and models are embodiments, not sources of meaning.

## 3. Canonical objects and state

The feature consumes current, versioned upstream records and emits typed outputs that remain linked to the active Harness, source package where applicable, Workflow Node, JIT Capsule, execution binding, evaluator, and receipt. Canonical records use stable serialization and immutable identities. A UI projection, model response, provider job, renderer workspace, or local cache cannot become accepted product state until its contract and authority gates pass.

Core invariants for this feature are:

- No fake artifacts count as release evidence.
- Format 02 is excluded.
- Implementation, evidence closure, readiness, and certification remain distinct.

## 4. Brownfield and external capability treatment

The implementation begins from exact current and predecessor evidence. The table below identifies the most relevant source records. `REUSE` or `ADAPT` permits bounded implementation reuse after namespace, authority, license, dependency, and behavior review; it never imports historical product meaning automatically.

| `SRC-AM-002` | `AMENDMENT_INPUT` | PA_AM_001_SEVEN_DAY_PARALLEL_PRODUCTION_ACTIVATION_V1_1(2).zip | Parallel Pipeline, temporal, static, VAE, Interview Expression, GNM, and retrieval/model-program activation lanes. |
| `SRC-EXT-017` | `REFERENCE` | github://browser-use/video-use | Packed phrase transcript, word-boundary EDL, FFmpeg correctness, rendered cut evaluation, bounded repair, and project memory. |
| `SRC-MIG-001` | `REFERENCE` | CMF_STUDIO_PREDECESSOR_MIGRATION_AUDIT_V1(1).md | Defines brownfield reuse/adapt/rewrite/archive treatment for the CMF Studio predecessor. |

## 5. Workflow integration

Validated upstream state → feature behavior → typed output and receipt → downstream handoff → evaluation, invalidation, and replay.

Every handoff is typed. A downstream node begins only after the producer output passes the declared contract and evidence gates. Failures are attributed to source, knowledge, retrieval, Skill, recipe, Programmed Model, tool, runtime, product, evaluator, or human-policy layers before repair or escalation.

## 6. Functional Requirements

### FR-115 — Build the source-first interview-to-content-batch reference slice

**Lifecycle:** `AMENDED_V1_1`  
**Normative requirement:** Release 1 shall admit one real Activative Interview or imported interview, produce an accepted Canonical Interview Source Package, launch a source-backed batch, render one talking-head A-roll short and one Carousel or SuperVisual from the same source, execute bounded evaluation and repair, record at least one HumanResolutionEpisode, and preserve exact source lineage.

**Trigger and preconditions:** Program Control authorizes the bounded Release 1 evidence campaign.

**Required output or state transition:** Real source package, content-batch plan, real short video, real static derivative, evaluation/repair receipts, human-resolution evidence, and audit bundle.

**Authority and invariants:**
- No fake URIs or synthetic assets count as real output.
- Talking-head A-roll remains the short’s base timeline.
- Format 02 is excluded.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given one accepted interview source, when the reference slice completes, then both outputs trace to exact source spans and pass technical, semantic, composition, and source-lineage gates.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given only a static synthetic fixture or a generated script with no interview source, when release evidence is assessed, then Release 1 remains incomplete.
- **Evidence required:** Real-file hashes, source-time maps, render/evaluation receipts, HumanResolutionEpisode, and operator acceptance.

**Governing decisions:** D039, D040, D041, D042, D043, D044, D054  
**Exact source references:** SRC-INT-001, SRC-AM-001, SRC-AM-002, SRC-EXT-017, SRC-MIG-001


### FR-116 — Require complete source-first release evidence

**Lifecycle:** `AMENDED_V1_1`  
**Normative requirement:** The Release 1 slice shall prove source rights and identity, dual-admission correctness, Harness and binding authority, retrieval relevance, program validity, renderer correctness, independent evaluation, local repair, human resolution capture, sandbox, cancellation/replay, fallback, and truthful claim ceilings.

**Trigger and preconditions:** Release readiness is evaluated.

**Required output or state transition:** A release evidence matrix, blockers, scope claims, and readiness receipt.

**Authority and invariants:**
- One happy path cannot certify the product.
- Implementation completion is not evidence closure.
- Human participant and source rights are explicit.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given the reference slice and required negative cases, when the matrix passes, then only the bounded source-first scope may be promoted.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given missing evaluator calibration or rights evidence, when readiness is computed, then production readiness remains false.
- **Evidence required:** Case-family reports, evaluator metrics, recovery/replay, rights/consent evidence, and release receipt.

**Governing decisions:** D039, D040, D054  
**Exact source references:** SRC-AM-001, SRC-AM-002, SRC-CUR-018, SRC-CUR-019


### FR-117 — Reconcile current repository and operator-local truth before implementation

**Lifecycle:** `AMENDED_V1_1`  
**Normative requirement:** Implementation shall not begin until public and operator-local Builder, VAE, Delegation, Studio predecessor, campaign-amendment, and source-crosswalk states are reconciled into one Program Control status without rewriting historical receipts.

**Trigger and preconditions:** The PRD or an implementation campaign seeks authorization.

**Required output or state transition:** One current status receipt, exact source hashes, resolved conflicts, and a bounded implementation allowlist.

**Authority and invariants:**
- Historical receipts remain immutable.
- Unverified local paths are not silently authoritative.
- All products consume the same current status.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given newer local terminal receipts, when verified, then Program Control publishes a superseding current status linked to both old and new evidence.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given operator-reported files that cannot be read or hashed, when reconciliation runs, then implementation remains blocked.
- **Evidence required:** Status reconciliation report, source manifests, conflict dispositions, and Program Control receipt.

**Governing decisions:** D039, D040, D054  
**Exact source references:** SRC-CUR-003, SRC-CUR-011, SRC-STATE-001, SRC-MIG-001, SRC-MIG-002


### FR-118 — Expand one source, category, runtime, provider, or learned claim boundary at a time

**Lifecycle:** `AMENDED_V1_1`  
**Normative requirement:** Every expansion beyond Release 1 shall declare its source-package requirements, category/profile, derivative contract, runtime or provider binding, learned claim envelope, evaluator profile, rights scope, rollback, and scope-specific evidence.

**Trigger and preconditions:** A team proposes a new profile, derivative, runtime, provider, model claim, or source type.

**Required output or state transition:** An expansion proposal, evidence cut, compatibility manifest, and bounded authorization decision.

**Authority and invariants:**
- No automatic inheritance of certification.
- Category identities remain distinct.
- New providers do not become product authority.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given a second short-video archetype, when proposed, then its source/sequence/evaluation differences and benchmark cases are explicit.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given a successful Carousel recipe, when reused for a SuperVisual without category evidence, then expansion is denied.
- **Evidence required:** Expansion manifest, benchmark/evaluation plan, compatibility tests, and authorization receipt.

**Governing decisions:** D039, D040, D054  
**Exact source references:** SRC-CUR-003, SRC-AM-001, SRC-AM-002


### FR-119 — Separate implementation, evidence closure, production readiness, and certification

**Lifecycle:** `AMENDED_V1_1`  
**Normative requirement:** Feature code, local tests, successful real outputs, production readiness, evaluator certification, and product certification shall remain separate claim states with independent evidence and authority.

**Trigger and preconditions:** Any status, UI, report, or release process describes completion.

**Required output or state transition:** A truthful claim-state projection and maximum supported claim.

**Authority and invariants:**
- Offline implementation cannot close real evidence gates.
- Capability presence cannot confer certification.
- Synthetic and real artifacts are distinct.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given a real render but no recovery evidence, when status is displayed, then it may claim a real bounded output but not production readiness.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given all unit tests pass, when a release report tries to claim certified, then claim-ceiling enforcement rejects it.
- **Evidence required:** Claim-state tests, evidence matrix, status receipts, and UI labeling checks.

**Governing decisions:** D039, D040, D054  
**Exact source references:** SRC-CUR-003, SRC-CUR-021, SRC-MIG-001


### FR-120 — Generate a bounded PRD-to-implementation handoff

**Lifecycle:** `AMENDED_V1_1`  
**Normative requirement:** After human ratification, the PRD shall produce a canonical FR ledger, value-based Epics, vertical CBAR-hardened Stories, Tech Spec candidates, exact source reuse dispositions, target paths, tests, evidence gates, Development Capsules, and authority boundaries without treating the planning package as implementation authorization.

**Trigger and preconditions:** The updated PRD passes structural and authority review.

**Required output or state transition:** Planning package, traceability matrices, candidate spec inventory, source allowlists, and next authorization request.

**Authority and invariants:**
- Every FR has one primary Story owner.
- Every Story names downstream failure and proof.
- Specs read exact brownfield files before design.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given the ratified PRD, when the planning factory runs, then all requirements map to one primary Story and candidate specs identify exact source paths and boundaries.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given an unmapped requirement or duplicate primary owner, when validation runs, then the handoff fails.
- **Evidence required:** Traceability validation, Story/FR ownership report, source-crosswalk validation, and planning receipt.

**Governing decisions:** D039, D040, D054  
**Exact source references:** SRC-MIG-001, SRC-MIG-002, SRC-TREE-001, SRC-SPEC-001

# F21 — Canonical Interview Source Package and Dual Admission

## 1. Product claim and user outcome

**User outcome:** Activative Interview sessions and imported interviews become equally valid, truthfully differentiated roots for downstream production.

Normalize video, transcript, speakers, times, rights, and provenance into one immutable source object without inventing missing Brief history. This feature exists to convert doctrine and source evidence into behavior that can be implemented, tested, denied, replayed, and audited. It does not grant implementation, provider, model-training, publication, production, or certification authority by itself.

## 2. Product boundary and ownership

Interview Expression owns source admission and package truth; Pipeline consumes the accepted package.

The feature must preserve the current product topology. Builder supplies the immutable Atomic Harness; Pipeline executes its declared nodes; Interview Expression owns source expression preparation and approval; VAE owns visual production; Delegation owns cross-product envelopes; Studio projects state and emits typed operator commands; Program Control owns cross-product authority and release truth. External renderers and models are embodiments, not sources of meaning.

## 3. Canonical objects and state

The feature consumes current, versioned upstream records and emits typed outputs that remain linked to the active Harness, source package where applicable, Workflow Node, JIT Capsule, execution binding, evaluator, and receipt. Canonical records use stable serialization and immutable identities. A UI projection, model response, provider job, renderer workspace, or local cache cannot become accepted product state until its contract and authority gates pass.

Core invariants for this feature are:

- Planned and actual expression are separate.
- Imported-source absence is explicit.
- Original media and history are immutable.

## 4. Brownfield and external capability treatment

The implementation begins from exact current and predecessor evidence. The table below identifies the most relevant source records. `REUSE` or `ADAPT` permits bounded implementation reuse after namespace, authority, license, dependency, and behavior review; it never imports historical product meaning automatically.

|---|---|---|---|

| `SRC-CUR-010` | `REFERENCE` | 01_ATOMIC_HARNESS_BUILDER/src/cmf_builder/workflow/actor_explicit_contracts.py | Execution-free Workflow Node, edge, authority and validation contracts. |

## 5. Workflow integration

Brief-led or imported source → technical and rights admission → transcript/speaker/time alignment → immutable Canonical Interview Source Package → downstream expression discovery.

Every handoff is typed. A downstream node begins only after the producer output passes the declared contract and evidence gates. Failures are attributed to source, knowledge, retrieval, Skill, recipe, Programmed Model, tool, runtime, product, evaluator, or human-policy layers before repair or escalation.

## 6. Functional Requirements

### FR-121 — Establish the Canonical Interview Source Package as the batch root

**Lifecycle:** `NEW_V1_1`  
**Normative requirement:** The product shall represent each interview-derived campaign with one immutable Canonical Interview Source Package that binds the accepted source media, transcript, speakers, timestamps, tags, Expression Moments, keyframes, rights, and provenance used by every derivative job.

**Trigger and preconditions:** An Activative Interview session completes or an existing interview is uploaded for production.

**Required output or state transition:** A stable source_package_id, version, manifest, source assets, transcript structures, evidence objects, rights scope, and downstream lineage root.

**Authority and invariants:**
- Every derivative references this root.
- The package records facts and evidence but does not itself create a content strategy.
- Original source bytes and historical versions remain immutable.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given an accepted interview and transcript, when the package is finalized, then a short-video, Carousel, and SuperVisual job can independently resolve the exact source objects they use.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given a derivative request with no accepted source_package_id, when batch admission runs, then the request is rejected as ungrounded.
- **Evidence required:** Package schema validation, source/hash manifest, lineage graph, and acceptance receipt.

**Governing decisions:** D041, D042, D044  
**Exact source references:** SRC-INT-001, SRC-INT-002, SRC-INT-003, SRC-AM-002


### FR-122 — Support Activative Interview Brief-led admission

**Lifecycle:** `NEW_V1_1`  
**Normative requirement:** The Interview Expression integration shall admit sessions produced from an Activative Interview Brief, preserving planned Context Premises, Matrix of Edging, anchors, Interview Asset Contracts, intended tags, consent, and session design separately from what the participant actually expressed.

**Trigger and preconditions:** An approved Activative Interview Brief and recording session are supplied.

**Required output or state transition:** A source package containing the Brief lineage, planned activation fields, recording assets, observed expression evidence, and planned-versus-observed comparison.

**Authority and invariants:**
- Planned intent is never represented as actual expression.
- Human reaction remains source evidence.
- Unsupported Brief expectations may remain unmet without fabrication.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given a Brief seeking a specific tension, when the interview does not produce it, then the package records the planned tag as unconfirmed and does not create an Expression Moment.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given a planned anchor with no matching source span, when downstream routing runs, then it cannot be used as quote or evidence.
- **Evidence required:** Brief hash, session consent, planned/observed tag comparison, and Interview Expression acceptance receipt.

**Governing decisions:** D041, D042, D045  
**Exact source references:** SRC-INT-001, SRC-INT-002, SRC-INT-003


### FR-123 — Support imported interview and transcript admission as a first-class path

**Lifecycle:** `NEW_V1_1`  
**Normative requirement:** The product shall admit an existing interview video with an uploaded or generated transcript without pretending that an Activative Interview Brief, Matrix of Edging, planned anchors, or predeclared asset contracts existed.

**Trigger and preconditions:** An operator uploads an interview or talking-head video and transcript, or requests transcription.

**Required output or state transition:** A source package with imported-source provenance, transcript/speaker alignment, retrospective evidence candidates, operator-confirmed context, and explicit absent-planning fields.

**Authority and invariants:**
- Imported sessions receive equal downstream production capability after validation.
- Missing upstream planning is disclosed, not synthesized.
- Retrospective inferences remain labeled until confirmed.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given a legacy interview with no Brief, when admitted, then the system can still produce a trusted source package and launch the same derivative Harnesses.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given a model-inferred Matrix of Edging represented as if it had guided the original interview, when validation runs, then the claim is rejected.
- **Evidence required:** Import receipt, source/transcript hashes, absent-field declaration, retrospective-tag evidence, and operator confirmation.

**Governing decisions:** D041, D042, D045  
**Exact source references:** SRC-INT-001, SRC-AM-002, SRC-EXT-017, SRC-EXT-023


### FR-124 — Align transcript, speakers, time bases, and media technically

**Lifecycle:** `NEW_V1_1`  
**Normative requirement:** The source-package compiler shall reconcile word-level timestamps, phrase boundaries, speaker diarization, audio events, source frame/time bases, media duration, and transcript confidence before source spans become eligible.

**Trigger and preconditions:** Source media and a transcript or transcription result are available.

**Required output or state transition:** Word and phrase records, speaker map, audio-event track, alignment confidence, source-time conversion functions, and blockers.

**Authority and invariants:**
- No source span exceeds media bounds.
- Speaker changes and phrase breaks are reproducible.
- Low-confidence regions remain visible.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given multi-speaker interview audio, when alignment completes, then every eligible phrase references one speaker and exact source times within tolerance.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given transcript drift beyond the declared tolerance, when Expression Moment extraction starts, then the affected ranges are blocked or routed for correction.
- **Evidence required:** Alignment benchmark, duration/time-base validation, diarization review samples, and phrase-pack hash.

**Governing decisions:** D041, D044  
**Exact source references:** SRC-EXT-017, SRC-EXT-020, SRC-EXT-023, SRC-INT-001


### FR-125 — Govern consent, rights, privacy, and derivative usage

**Lifecycle:** `NEW_V1_1`  
**Normative requirement:** The source package shall declare participant consent, ownership, allowed derivative formats, publication scope, model-training eligibility, identity/voice use, retention, withdrawal, and restricted evidence before any job or learning disposition is admitted.

**Trigger and preconditions:** Source material enters the workspace or its permitted use changes.

**Required output or state transition:** A versioned rights-and-consent envelope linked to source assets, derivatives, training eligibility, and withdrawal/invalidation policy.

**Authority and invariants:**
- No job exceeds the granted scope.
- Training rights are independent from production rights.
- Withdrawal preserves audit history while preventing new prohibited use.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given consent for social derivatives but not model training, when the content batch runs, then production may proceed while dataset compilation excludes the source.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given expired or withdrawn publication authority, when a publish command runs, then it is denied and affected unpublished derivatives are blocked.
- **Evidence required:** Consent receipts, policy tests, usage audit, withdrawal simulation, and rights-filter results.

**Governing decisions:** D041, D044, D047  
**Exact source references:** SRC-INT-001, SRC-AM-001


### FR-126 — Version, supersede, and invalidate source packages safely

**Lifecycle:** `NEW_V1_1`  
**Normative requirement:** Corrections to transcripts, speakers, tags, rights, Expression Moments, or source assets shall create a new immutable source-package version and compute selective downstream invalidation rather than rewriting accepted history.

**Trigger and preconditions:** An operator or validator corrects an accepted source-package field or a right/authority state changes.

**Required output or state transition:** A superseding package version, field-level change set, affected-job graph, invalidation proposals, and historical reproduction path.

**Authority and invariants:**
- Original package versions remain reproducible.
- Only dependent derivatives are invalidated.
- Human decisions are never regenerated during replay.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given a corrected speaker assignment in one phrase, when supersession occurs, then only derivatives using that phrase are invalidated.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given a corrected transcript, when a service mutates the original package in place, then integrity validation fails.
- **Evidence required:** Version/hash comparison, dependency analysis, selective invalidation tests, and historical replay.

**Governing decisions:** D041, D044, D047  
**Exact source references:** SRC-CUR-010, SRC-AM-001, SRC-AM-002


## 7. Execution, model, tool, and human responsibilities

Deterministic services own mechanically decidable facts. Programmed Models or bounded Agent Programs may propose or compile behavior only within their evidence-backed claim and node-local tool grants. Independent evaluators inspect judgment dimensions. Humans own new meaning, consent, identity, unresolved taste, policy exceptions, promotion, and publication authority where assigned. The producing model or runtime cannot accept its own output.

When the feature uses a Hunter, Analyst, Composer, or Commander role, the role is an explicit workflow responsibility. It may be implemented by code, a small model, a larger model, or a human. The role name never hides the actual actor or expand its authority.

## 8. Validation and quality gates

Validation must prove both the intended result and the process that produced it. The minimum feature evidence includes dual-admission tests, source/transcript alignment, rights, versioning, supersession, and source-package receipts. Mechanical tests run before expensive model or visual evaluation. Judgment evaluators are calibrated to the exact category and context. Every denial names the cause, owner, and next admissible action. Every accepted mutation emits an immutable receipt and updates only dependent state.

## 9. Risks, mitigations, and stop conditions

| Risk | Concrete consequence | Mitigation |
|---|---|---|
| Authority drift | A predecessor, external project, UI, model, or renderer is treated as current product authority. | Require exact source disposition, current authority validation, and product-boundary tests. |
| False completion | A synthetic URI, dry-run, unverified command, or model self-report is promoted as a real result. | Require actual files, hashes, independent validation, and artifact-class labels. |
| Over-broad automation | A model or agent gains tools, context, or authority beyond the current node. | Use JIT context, node-local tool grants, sandboxes, and explicit escalation. |
| Hidden mutation | Accepted meaning, source, program, or human preference changes without a versioned record. | Use immutable versions, typed commands, receipts, and selective invalidation. |
| Source truth loss | A derived artifact, route, quote, or cut weakens or changes the participant's actual expression. | Require exact source context, quote/voice labels, independent semantic review, and downstream lineage. |

**Stop conditions**

- The behavior would create a second semantic or canonical state owner.
- A required source, right, authority, contract, runtime, evaluator, or human decision is unavailable or unverified.
- The implementation would treat migration evidence or an external project as current authority.
- The change would imply real output, production readiness, or certification beyond available evidence.

## 10. Planning and implementation handoff

This module is implementation-ready only after its FRs have one primary vertical Story owner, its Stories pass CBAR hardening, its candidate Tech Specs identify exact existing code and target paths, and Program Control issues a bounded Development Capsule. Until then, this module is a product-authority draft.

*This feature module belongs to the Conscious Activations Atomic Harness Pipeline PRD V1.1 source-first reconciliation package.*


---

# F22 — Activative Tags, Expression Moments, Keyframes, and Asset Package Spec

## 1. Product claim and user outcome

**User outcome:** The source becomes a compact, inspectable inventory of approved expression material, visual references, and routeable ingredients.

Separate tag provenance, pack transcript context, map shots/keyframes, govern Moment discovery, retain negatives, and compile downstream handoff. This feature exists to convert doctrine and source evidence into behavior that can be implemented, tested, denied, replayed, and audited. It does not grant implementation, provider, model-training, publication, production, or certification authority by itself.

## 2. Product boundary and ownership

Interview Expression owns discovery and approval; Pipeline consumes the Asset Package Spec.

The feature must preserve the current product topology. Builder supplies the immutable Atomic Harness; Pipeline executes its declared nodes; Interview Expression owns source expression preparation and approval; VAE owns visual production; Delegation owns cross-product envelopes; Studio projects state and emits typed operator commands; Program Control owns cross-product authority and release truth. External renderers and models are embodiments, not sources of meaning.

## 3. Canonical objects and state

The feature consumes current, versioned upstream records and emits typed outputs that remain linked to the active Harness, source package where applicable, Workflow Node, JIT Capsule, execution binding, evaluator, and receipt. Canonical records use stable serialization and immutable identities. A UI projection, model response, provider job, renderer workspace, or local cache cannot become accepted product state until its contract and authority gates pass.

Core invariants for this feature are:

- Hunters propose but do not approve.
- Every quote and moment has exact source context.
- Rejected evidence remains excluded but learnable within rights.

## 4. Brownfield and external capability treatment

The implementation begins from exact current and predecessor evidence. The table below identifies the most relevant source records. `REUSE` or `ADAPT` permits bounded implementation reuse after namespace, authority, license, dependency, and behavior review; it never imports historical product meaning automatically.

| Source | Disposition | Exact path or reference | Role |
|---|---|---|---|
| `SRC-INT-002` | `ADAPT` | THE_CMF_STUDIO(2).zip::CCP V9 Interview-First Expression Engine.md | Expression capture, source truth, archetype routing, and interview-first doctrine. |
| `SRC-INT-003` | `ADAPT` | THE_CMF_STUDIO(2).zip::CCP V9.1 Expression Capture & Archetype Routing Update.md | Expression Moment and archetype-routing refinements. |
| `SRC-AM-002` | `AMENDMENT_INPUT` | PA_AM_001_SEVEN_DAY_PARALLEL_PRODUCTION_ACTIVATION_V1_1(2).zip | Parallel Pipeline, temporal, static, VAE, Interview Expression, GNM, and retrieval/model-program activation lanes. |
| `SRC-EXT-017` | `REFERENCE` | github://browser-use/video-use | Packed phrase transcript, word-boundary EDL, FFmpeg correctness, rendered cut evaluation, bounded repair, and project memory. |
| `SRC-EXT-023` | `REFERENCE` | github://SamurAIGPT/AI-Youtube-Shorts-Generator | Long-video chunking with overlap, deduplication, caching, structured JSON, and vertical crop patterns. |
| `SRC-INT-001` | `ADAPT` | THE_CMF_STUDIO(2).zip::05_PRD_CMF_STUDIO_INTERVIEW_FIRST.md | Interview-first source-to-asset product model and Complete Expression Session concepts. |
| `SRC-EXT-020` | `REFERENCE` | github://UVA-Computer-Vision-Lab/OmniShotCut | Shot-boundary and transition classification. |
| `SRC-AM-001` | `AMENDMENT_INPUT` | CONSCIOUS_ACTIVATIONS_STUDIO_ARCHITECTURE_AMENDMENT_V2_1(2).zip | Format 02 deferral, HumanResolutionEpisode, supervisory Studio, autonomy modes, timeline adoption, and Revision Compiler. |

## 5. Workflow integration

Accepted source package → tag/phrase/shot/keyframe analysis → Hunter proposals → Analyst validation → approval/rejection → Expression Ingredient Inventory and Asset Package Spec.

Every handoff is typed. A downstream node begins only after the producer output passes the declared contract and evidence gates. Failures are attributed to source, knowledge, retrieval, Skill, recipe, Programmed Model, tool, runtime, product, evaluator, or human-policy layers before repair or escalation.

## 6. Functional Requirements

### FR-127 — Separate planned, observed, inferred, confirmed, rejected, and superseded tags

**Lifecycle:** `NEW_V1_1`  
**Normative requirement:** Every source and routing tag shall declare its provenance state, evidence, confidence, authority, applicability, and lifecycle so an intended interview topic cannot be confused with an observed Expression Moment or an operator-confirmed route.

**Trigger and preconditions:** A Brief, transcript analysis, source observation, operator decision, or supersession produces a tag.

**Required output or state transition:** Typed tag records and relationships to source spans, evidence, Brief items, archetypes, and downstream jobs.

**Authority and invariants:**
- Tag states never collapse silently.
- Inference cannot outrank confirmed evidence.
- Rejected tags remain available as negative evidence.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given a planned 'authority conflict' tag and an observed unrelated answer, when routing runs, then only observed/confirmed tags influence the job unless the operator resolves the gap.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given an inferred tag with no supporting source span, when it is proposed for a quote card, then eligibility fails.
- **Evidence required:** Tag-state registry tests, provenance graph, evidence links, and exclusion receipt.

**Governing decisions:** D045  
**Exact source references:** SRC-INT-002, SRC-INT-003, SRC-AM-002


### FR-128 — Use the packed phrase-level transcript as the primary language reasoning surface

**Lifecycle:** `NEW_V1_1`  
**Normative requirement:** The Pipeline shall compile a compact, speaker-aware, time-annotated phrase transcript from cached word-level data and use it as the default text reasoning surface, loading raw words or visual composites only when the current decision requires them.

**Trigger and preconditions:** Transcript alignment is accepted.

**Required output or state transition:** A versioned phrase pack with source IDs, start/end times, speaker, words, audio events, tags, and links to source evidence.

**Authority and invariants:**
- Raw word data remains canonical for timing.
- Compression cannot remove editorially meaningful fillers or events without declaration.
- Phrase packing is deterministic.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given a one-hour interview, when a Moment Hunter runs, then it receives the compact phrase pack plus only the relevant raw words and visual evidence.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given phrase packing that normalizes away a hesitation used as an expression signal, when validation compares it with raw ASR, then the pack is rejected.
- **Evidence required:** Phrase-pack hash, compression coverage, source-word backreferences, and retrieval/context-size benchmark.

**Governing decisions:** D041, D053  
**Exact source references:** SRC-EXT-017, SRC-EXT-023, SRC-INT-001


### FR-129 — Build source shot maps, transitions, keyframes, and visual references

**Lifecycle:** `NEW_V1_1`  
**Normative requirement:** The source-package compiler shall detect existing shot boundaries and transitions, sample representative and expression-relevant keyframes, record camera/framing changes, and expose visual references without treating shot changes as semantic importance.

**Trigger and preconditions:** Video source media passes technical admission.

**Required output or state transition:** A shot map, transition labels, keyframe set, visual-quality notes, face/subject geometry where available, and source-time references.

**Authority and invariants:**
- Shot detection does not create Expression Moments.
- Keyframes remain linked to exact source frames.
- Model uncertainty and missed-transition risk are visible.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given an already edited interview, when shot analysis runs, then downstream edit planning can avoid cutting across source dissolves and can retrieve representative frames.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given a detected shot boundary, when no meaningful expression or quote exists, then it is not automatically routed as content.
- **Evidence required:** Detection benchmark, frame hashes, source-time validation, and sampled human review.

**Governing decisions:** D041, D044, D053  
**Exact source references:** SRC-EXT-020, SRC-EXT-017, SRC-INT-001


### FR-130 — Discover and approve Anchor Hits and Expression Moments

**Lifecycle:** `NEW_V1_1`  
**Normative requirement:** A bounded Expression Moment Hunter may propose source-backed spans using transcript, audio events, keyframes, Brief context, tags, and evidence; an Analyst validates truth and completeness, and only the authorized approval path may promote an Expression Moment.

**Trigger and preconditions:** An accepted source package is ready for expression discovery.

**Required output or state transition:** Candidate Anchor Hits and Expression Moments with source spans, quotes, speakers, evidence, expression qualities, archetype opportunities, confidence, and verdicts.

**Authority and invariants:**
- The Hunter cannot approve, route, or invent unsupported quotes.
- Expression meaning remains source-backed.
- Rejected candidates remain historical.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given a charged answer with a complete premise and reaction tail, when proposed and validated, then it may become an approved Expression Moment with exact source lineage.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given a catchy partial quote that reverses the speaker's meaning outside context, when the Analyst checks it, then promotion is denied.
- **Evidence required:** Candidate portfolio, source-context review, Analyst report, approval receipt, and false-positive/false-negative benchmark.

**Governing decisions:** D041, D045, D052  
**Exact source references:** SRC-INT-001, SRC-INT-002, SRC-INT-003, SRC-AM-002


### FR-131 — Preserve rejected and borderline expression evidence

**Lifecycle:** `NEW_V1_1`  
**Normative requirement:** Rejected, incomplete, unsafe, low-confidence, or borderline Anchor Hit and Expression Moment candidates shall be stored with reasons, responsible failure layer, and future admissibility conditions rather than discarded.

**Trigger and preconditions:** Expression candidate evaluation returns other than accepted.

**Required output or state transition:** A rejected/borderline evidence record linked to source spans, verdict dimensions, reviewer, and possible repair or re-evaluation condition.

**Authority and invariants:**
- Rejected evidence cannot enter production routing.
- Negative examples remain rights-scoped.
- A later superseding decision is additive.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given a powerful quote with insufficient consent for publication, when evaluated, then it remains a restricted candidate and cannot enter a content job.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given a rejected candidate, when retrieval searches for production-ready moments, then it is excluded but may appear as required negative evidence.
- **Evidence required:** Lifecycle and retrieval tests, rejection reasons, rights scope, and supersession history.

**Governing decisions:** D045, D047  
**Exact source references:** SRC-INT-001, SRC-AM-001


### FR-132 — Compile an Expression Ingredient Inventory and Asset Package Spec

**Lifecycle:** `NEW_V1_1`  
**Normative requirement:** Interview Expression shall compile approved quotes, evidence, Expression Moments, keyframes, voice/audio references, visual references, tags, archetype opportunities, restrictions, and lineage into an Asset Package Spec that downstream Atomic Harnesses can consume without rediscovering the source.

**Trigger and preconditions:** Expression discovery and source validation reach an approved handoff state.

**Required output or state transition:** A versioned Expression Ingredient Inventory and Asset Package Spec linked to the Canonical Interview Source Package.

**Authority and invariants:**
- The package exposes possibilities, not final derivative meaning.
- Each ingredient carries source and authority.
- Unavailable or restricted ingredients remain explicit.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given an approved session, when the package is compiled, then a short-video and Carousel Harness can select ingredients with no loss of source-time or evidence lineage.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given a quote without exact words or source time, when the package is validated, then it is rejected.
- **Evidence required:** Schema validation, completeness report, ingredient/source graph, restrictions, and handoff receipt.

**Governing decisions:** D041, D044, D046  
**Exact source references:** SRC-INT-001, SRC-INT-002, SRC-INT-003, SRC-AM-002


## 7. Execution, model, tool, and human responsibilities

Deterministic services own mechanically decidable facts. Programmed Models or bounded Agent Programs may propose or compile behavior only within their evidence-backed claim and node-local tool grants. Independent evaluators inspect judgment dimensions. Humans own new meaning, consent, identity, unresolved taste, policy exceptions, promotion, and publication authority where assigned. The producing model or runtime cannot accept its own output.

When the feature uses a Hunter, Analyst, Composer, or Commander role, the role is an explicit workflow responsibility. It may be implemented by code, a small model, a larger model, or a human. The role name never hides the actual actor or expand its authority.

## 8. Validation and quality gates

# F23 — Source-Backed Content Batch and Archetype Routing

## 1. Product claim and user outcome

**User outcome:** One source package launches a coordinated set of eligible derivative Harness jobs with shared analysis and exact lineage.

Compile batch programs, rank supported archetypes, create immutable derivative jobs, reuse source analysis, represent bounded roles, and selectively invalidate. This feature exists to convert doctrine and source evidence into behavior that can be implemented, tested, denied, replayed, and audited. It does not grant implementation, provider, model-training, publication, production, or certification authority by itself.

## 2. Product boundary and ownership

Pipeline owns batch compilation and execution; each derivative Harness remains Builder-defined.

The feature must preserve the current product topology. Builder supplies the immutable Atomic Harness; Pipeline executes its declared nodes; Interview Expression owns source expression preparation and approval; VAE owns visual production; Delegation owns cross-product envelopes; Studio projects state and emits typed operator commands; Program Control owns cross-product authority and release truth. External renderers and models are embodiments, not sources of meaning.

## 3. Canonical objects and state

The feature consumes current, versioned upstream records and emits typed outputs that remain linked to the active Harness, source package where applicable, Workflow Node, JIT Capsule, execution binding, evaluator, and receipt. Canonical records use stable serialization and immutable identities. A UI projection, model response, provider job, renderer workspace, or local cache cannot become accepted product state until its contract and authority gates pass.

Core invariants for this feature are:

- No route is manufactured.
- Each job has its own Harness and evidence.
- Shared changes invalidate only dependents.

## 4. Brownfield and external capability treatment

The implementation begins from exact current and predecessor evidence. The table below identifies the most relevant source records. `REUSE` or `ADAPT` permits bounded implementation reuse after namespace, authority, license, dependency, and behavior review; it never imports historical product meaning automatically.

| Source | Disposition | Exact path or reference | Role |
|---|---|---|---|
| `SRC-AM-001` | `AMENDMENT_INPUT` | CONSCIOUS_ACTIVATIONS_STUDIO_ARCHITECTURE_AMENDMENT_V2_1(2).zip | Format 02 deferral, HumanResolutionEpisode, supervisory Studio, autonomy modes, timeline adoption, and Revision Compiler. |
| `SRC-AM-002` | `AMENDMENT_INPUT` | PA_AM_001_SEVEN_DAY_PARALLEL_PRODUCTION_ACTIVATION_V1_1(2).zip | Parallel Pipeline, temporal, static, VAE, Interview Expression, GNM, and retrieval/model-program activation lanes. |
| `SRC-INT-001` | `ADAPT` | THE_CMF_STUDIO(2).zip::05_PRD_CMF_STUDIO_INTERVIEW_FIRST.md | Interview-first source-to-asset product model and Complete Expression Session concepts. |
| `SRC-INT-003` | `ADAPT` | THE_CMF_STUDIO(2).zip::CCP V9.1 Expression Capture & Archetype Routing Update.md | Expression Moment and archetype-routing refinements. |
| `SRC-CUR-004` | `REFERENCE` | 01_ATOMIC_HARNESS_BUILDER/src/cmf_builder/domain/atomic_harness_definition.py | Canonical AtomicHarnessDefinition structure and execution-free status. |
| `SRC-CUR-007` | `REFERENCE` | 01_ATOMIC_HARNESS_BUILDER/src/cmf_builder/domain/category_runtime_rules.py | Category-native runtime plan requirements, evaluation dimensions and repair units. |
| `SRC-EXT-023` | `REFERENCE` | github://SamurAIGPT/AI-Youtube-Shorts-Generator | Long-video chunking with overlap, deduplication, caching, structured JSON, and vertical crop patterns. |
| `SRC-MIG-001` | `REFERENCE` | CMF_STUDIO_PREDECESSOR_MIGRATION_AUDIT_V1(1).md | Defines brownfield reuse/adapt/rewrite/archive treatment for the CMF Studio predecessor. |
| `SRC-CUR-010` | `REFERENCE` | 01_ATOMIC_HARNESS_BUILDER/src/cmf_builder/workflow/actor_explicit_contracts.py | Execution-free Workflow Node, edge, authority and validation contracts. |

## 5. Workflow integration

Source or Asset Package Spec → target outputs → archetype and Harness eligibility → immutable derivative jobs → explicit role/node graph → coordinated batch execution.

Every handoff is typed. A downstream node begins only after the producer output passes the declared contract and evidence gates. Failures are attributed to source, knowledge, retrieval, Skill, recipe, Programmed Model, tool, runtime, product, evaluator, or human-policy layers before repair or escalation.

## 6. Functional Requirements

### FR-133 — Compile one source-backed content-batch program

**Lifecycle:** `NEW_V1_1`  
**Normative requirement:** The Pipeline shall compile a Content Batch Orchestration Program from one accepted source package or Asset Package Spec, declaring target derivative jobs, Harnesses, shared ingredients, dependencies, budgets, deadlines, review modes, and source-lineage obligations.

**Trigger and preconditions:** An operator selects a source package, objectives, target outputs, and approved Harnesses.

**Required output or state transition:** A versioned batch program and job graph for short videos, Carousels, SuperVisuals, animation derivatives, or other authorized outputs.

**Authority and invariants:**
- The batch does not change source meaning.
- Each job remains independently cancelable and attributable.
- Shared dependencies are explicit.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given one interview and a request for two shorts plus one Carousel, when compiled, then the jobs share source analysis while preserving separate Harness and evaluation requirements.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given an output type with no current Harness, when batch compilation runs, then that job is blocked without blocking unrelated eligible jobs.
- **Evidence required:** Batch schema, dependency graph, budget plan, Harness binding validation, and compilation receipt.

**Governing decisions:** D046  
**Exact source references:** SRC-AM-001, SRC-AM-002, SRC-INT-001


### FR-134 — Route approved expression material through eligible archetypes and Harnesses

**Lifecycle:** `NEW_V1_1`  
**Normative requirement:** Archetype routing shall rank only current, category-eligible, source-supported routes using approved Expression Moments, tags, audience/context evidence, target platform, and Harness availability; it shall expose alternatives and never manufacture a fit.

**Trigger and preconditions:** An Asset Package Spec and target content objectives are available.

**Required output or state transition:** Ranked route proposals with source support, expected viewer function, required ingredients, exclusions, and selected Harness identity.

**Authority and invariants:**
- Archetype route is not source truth.
- Wrong-category and unsupported routes are excluded before ranking.
- Human creative authority may resolve genuine alternatives.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given an Expression Moment that supports a myth-debunk sequence, when routing runs, then it proposes the matching current short-video Harness and explains evidence.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given a strong quote that lacks the evidence needed by a data-story route, when routing runs, then that route is excluded.
- **Evidence required:** Eligibility tests, route ranking benchmark, exclusion reasons, and route-selection receipt.

**Governing decisions:** D045, D046, D052  
**Exact source references:** SRC-INT-003, SRC-AM-002


### FR-135 — Create immutable derivative job contracts

**Lifecycle:** `NEW_V1_1`  
**Normative requirement:** Each batch job shall bind one Harness version, exact source-package and ingredient references, derivative type, target platform/profile, intended Activative and sequence function, output constraints, runtime capabilities, evaluation, rights, and review policy.

**Trigger and preconditions:** A batch route is selected.

**Required output or state transition:** An immutable ContentDerivativeJob contract and dependency links.

**Authority and invariants:**
- Jobs cannot read arbitrary source material outside their grant.
- Job intent and source references are separately versioned.
- Execution binding cannot mutate the contract.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given a source-led short job, when admitted, then it contains exact source spans or a bounded selection contract and the talking-head A-roll rule.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given a job whose requested platform exceeds rights scope, when admitted, then it is rejected before execution.
- **Evidence required:** Job schema, authority/rights filters, source-grant validation, and admission receipt.

**Governing decisions:** D044, D046  
**Exact source references:** SRC-CUR-004, SRC-CUR-007, SRC-AM-002


### FR-136 — Share source analysis while preventing duplicate or conflicting derivatives

**Lifecycle:** `NEW_V1_1`  
**Normative requirement:** The batch runtime shall reuse accepted source transcripts, phrase packs, shot maps, keyframes, and approved moments, deduplicate overlapping derivative candidates, and detect conflicting source uses or near-duplicate outputs before production spend.

**Trigger and preconditions:** Multiple jobs or candidate routes use the same source package.

**Required output or state transition:** Shared read-only source-analysis bindings, deduplication groups, conflict warnings, and accepted diversity plan.

**Authority and invariants:**
- Shared analysis is immutable.
- Deduplication does not erase distinct archetype purposes.
- Conflicts are explicit.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given two proposed shorts using more than the allowed source overlap for the same hook, when batch planning runs, then the system keeps the stronger or requires a differentiated route.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given identical transcript analysis requested by three jobs, when scheduled, then it is reused rather than rerun.
- **Evidence required:** Reuse-cache tests, overlap/dedupe report, diversity evidence, and cost savings receipt.

**Governing decisions:** D046  
**Exact source references:** SRC-EXT-023, SRC-AM-002


### FR-137 — Represent Hunters, Analysts, Composers, and Commanders as bounded workflow roles

**Lifecycle:** `NEW_V1_1`  
**Normative requirement:** The Pipeline shall model Hunter, Analyst, Composer, and Commander responsibilities as explicit node roles with separate capabilities, tools, inputs, outputs, authority, and failure handling rather than hidden personas or a monolithic multi-agent prompt.

**Trigger and preconditions:** A Harness compiles a source-discovery, evaluation, composition, or gate responsibility.

**Required output or state transition:** Role-labeled Workflow Nodes and typed handoffs mapped to actual execution actors.

**Authority and invariants:**
- Role is independent from model or service identity.
- Hunters do not approve; Composers do not self-evaluate; Commanders authorize only assigned transitions.
- Deterministic implementations may fill roles.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given Expression Moment discovery, when the workflow compiles, then Hunter proposals flow to an Analyst and an authorized approval node before routing.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given a single model configured to hunt, compose, approve, and evaluate its own output, when ownership validation runs, then the graph is rejected.
- **Evidence required:** Role/actor taxonomy tests, handoff contracts, authority matrix, and node receipts.

**Governing decisions:** D052  
**Exact source references:** SRC-MIG-001, SRC-INT-001, SRC-CUR-010


### FR-138 — Propagate source or batch changes through selective invalidation

**Lifecycle:** `NEW_V1_1`  
**Normative requirement:** When a source package, approved moment, route, rights state, Harness, or shared ingredient is superseded, the batch runtime shall compute and rerun only affected jobs and descendants while preserving accepted unaffected work.

**Trigger and preconditions:** A shared upstream object changes or is revoked.

**Required output or state transition:** Dependency impact report, invalidation events, preserved checkpoints, rerun plan, and operator notification.

**Authority and invariants:**
- No blanket regeneration without dependency evidence.
- Revoked rights block new use immediately.
- Historical outputs remain auditable.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given one Expression Moment quote correction, when superseded, then only derivatives that use it are invalidated.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given an unrelated keyframe correction, when a short uses no such frame, then its accepted render remains valid.
- **Evidence required:** Dependency-graph tests, invalidation receipts, checkpoint reuse, and historical audit.

**Governing decisions:** D044, D046, D047  
**Exact source references:** SRC-CUR-010, SRC-AM-001, SRC-AM-002


## 7. Execution, model, tool, and human responsibilities

Deterministic services own mechanically decidable facts. Programmed Models or bounded Agent Programs may propose or compile behavior only within their evidence-backed claim and node-local tool grants. Independent evaluators inspect judgment dimensions. Humans own new meaning, consent, identity, unresolved taste, policy exceptions, promotion, and publication authority where assigned. The producing model or runtime cannot accept its own output.

When the feature uses a Hunter, Analyst, Composer, or Commander role, the role is an explicit workflow responsibility. It may be implemented by code, a small model, a larger model, or a human. The role name never hides the actual actor or expand its authority.

## 8. Validation and quality gates

The minimum feature evidence includes batch graph, route eligibility benchmark, job contracts, dedupe/diversity, role/actor tests, and invalidation. Mechanical tests run before expensive model or visual evaluation. Judgment evaluators are calibrated to the exact category and context. |---|---|---|
