**Requirement:** Planned interview intent, observed expression, model inference, operator confirmation, rejection, and supersession remain distinct states.

**Verification:** Contract tests, source/authority evidence, behavior-specific integration tests, and immutable receipts.

### NFR-SRC-003

**Requirement:** Every eligible word, phrase, Expression Moment, keyframe, quote, and derivative resolves to exact source identity and time/frame ranges.

**Verification:** Contract tests, source/authority evidence, behavior-specific integration tests, and immutable receipts.

### NFR-SRC-004

**Requirement:** Consent, rights, privacy, identity, voice, publication, training, retention, and withdrawal policies are enforced before retrieval, execution, export, and learning.

**Verification:** Contract tests, source/authority evidence, behavior-specific integration tests, and immutable receipts.

### NFR-SRC-005

**Requirement:** Transcript, speaker, shot, and source corrections create new versions and selective invalidation rather than in-place mutation.

**Verification:** Contract tests, source/authority evidence, behavior-specific integration tests, and immutable receipts.

### NFR-BATCH-001

**Requirement:** One source package may feed multiple derivative jobs without duplicating accepted source analysis.

**Verification:** Contract tests, source/authority evidence, behavior-specific integration tests, and immutable receipts.

### NFR-BATCH-002

**Requirement:** Every derivative job has one explicit Harness, category/profile, source grant, runtime binding, evaluator, and review policy.

**Verification:** Contract tests, source/authority evidence, behavior-specific integration tests, and immutable receipts.

### NFR-BATCH-003

**Requirement:** Talking-head footage and source audio remain the A-roll spine for source-led short-video jobs.

**Verification:** Contract tests, source/authority evidence, behavior-specific integration tests, and immutable receipts.

### NFR-BATCH-004

**Requirement:** Carousels, SuperVisuals, and animation derivatives preserve source/evidence lineage even when the original footage is absent from the final artifact.

**Verification:** Contract tests, source/authority evidence, behavior-specific integration tests, and immutable receipts.

### NFR-BATCH-005

**Requirement:** Batch changes invalidate only dependent jobs and preserve unrelated accepted work.

**Verification:** Contract tests, source/authority evidence, behavior-specific integration tests, and immutable receipts.

### NFR-REV-001

**Requirement:** Natural-language revisions and direct manipulation use one typed ChangeRequestProgram path.

**Verification:** Contract tests, source/authority evidence, behavior-specific integration tests, and immutable receipts.

### NFR-REV-002

**Requirement:** Every accepted revision is the smallest authority-valid change that preserves already-valid relationships.

**Verification:** Contract tests, source/authority evidence, behavior-specific integration tests, and immutable receipts.

### NFR-REV-003

**Requirement:** Every meaningful human decision emits a complete, attributable HumanResolutionEpisode.

**Verification:** Contract tests, source/authority evidence, behavior-specific integration tests, and immutable receipts.

### NFR-REV-004

**Requirement:** Human-resolution capture and retrieval indexing are automatic, while model, Skill, recipe, and doctrine promotion remain offline, evaluated, reversible, and human-authorized.

**Verification:** Contract tests, source/authority evidence, behavior-specific integration tests, and immutable receipts.

### NFR-REV-005

**Requirement:** Revision and repair loops stop by configured limits and escalate unresolved human-owned boundaries.

**Verification:** Contract tests, source/authority evidence, behavior-specific integration tests, and immutable receipts.

### NFR-STU-001

**Requirement:** Studio UI and category modules are projections and typed command surfaces, never canonical workflow, source, composition, or timeline stores.

**Verification:** Contract tests, source/authority evidence, behavior-specific integration tests, and immutable receipts.

### NFR-STU-002

**Requirement:** Autonomy modes enforce exactly which human gates and publication actions are permitted.

**Verification:** Contract tests, source/authority evidence, behavior-specific integration tests, and immutable receipts.

### NFR-STU-003

**Requirement:** Operators receive exception packages containing cause, source, evidence, alternatives, authority, cost, downstream impact, and allowed actions.

**Verification:** Contract tests, source/authority evidence, behavior-specific integration tests, and immutable receipts.

### NFR-STU-004

**Requirement:** Realtime read models disclose freshness, artifact class, and authority status.

**Verification:** Contract tests, source/authority evidence, behavior-specific integration tests, and immutable receipts.

### NFR-STU-005

**Requirement:** Category Studio plugins expose only commands and evidence granted by the active Harness and product boundaries.

**Verification:** Contract tests, source/authority evidence, behavior-specific integration tests, and immutable receipts.

### NFR-VAE-001

**Requirement:** SAM3, Lucida, layered providers, ComfyUI, GNM, and visual production strategies remain VAE-owned.

**Verification:** Contract tests, source/authority evidence, behavior-specific integration tests, and immutable receipts.

### NFR-VAE-002

**Requirement:** GNM identity and expression parameters are geometric controls and must not be represented as human identity or emotional truth.

**Verification:** Contract tests, source/authority evidence, behavior-specific integration tests, and immutable receipts.

### NFR-VAE-003

**Requirement:** Real-person GNM use requires approved source references or fitting evidence; demographic identity sampling is prohibited as identity authority.

**Verification:** Contract tests, source/authority evidence, behavior-specific integration tests, and immutable receipts.

### NFR-F02-001

**Requirement:** No active Format 02 runtime, Studio route, benchmark, Programmed Model claim, production claim, or certification exists before the current Harness activation gate.

**Verification:** Contract tests, source/authority evidence, behavior-specific integration tests, and immutable receipts.

### NFR-EXT-001

**Requirement:** External projects contribute bounded capability evidence only after license, security, architecture, and contract review; they never become semantic authority.

**Verification:** Contract tests, source/authority evidence, behavior-specific integration tests, and immutable receipts.

# Categories, Sources, Formats, and Runtime Scope

| Category / profile | Current authority state | Source rule | Runtime path | Release posture |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| `short_form_edited_video` / current registered formats 01, 03–08 | Current Builder profile identities; profile evidence still required per release | Interview-derived jobs consume the Canonical Interview Source Package and preserve talking-head A-roll for source-led shorts | VideoEditProgram → FFmpeg / Remotion master / HyperFrames child slots or eligible master | Release 1 proves one bounded source-led path |
| `carousels` / profile IDs pending current ratification | Category registered; predecessor workspace identities are evidence only | Quotes, evidence, Expression Moments, keyframes, and editorial transformations preserve source lineage | Carousel Composition IR → PRETEXT / geometry / Skia | One source-grounded Carousel may satisfy the static Release 1 derivative |
| `supervisuals` / profile IDs pending current ratification | Category registered; predecessor workspace identities are evidence only | One approved premise, proof, quote, or invitation with exact source/evidence lineage | Single-frame Composition IR → PRETEXT / geometry / Skia | One source-grounded SuperVisual may satisfy the static Release 1 derivative |
| separately authorized non-Format-02 2D animation derivative | Requires its own current Harness and runtime binding | May use source audio, voiceover derivatives, quotes, evidence, keyframes, and identity references | Animation program → HyperFrames / Remotion / Stretchy-Spine or another approved embodiment | Expansion after bounded authority and evidence |
| `format02_minimal_coach_theatre` | **DEFERRED_AWAITING_CURRENT_ATOMIC_HARNESS** | Historical registries and prototypes are evidence only | No active runtime or Studio binding | Excluded from Release 1 and active implementation |
| `interview_expression` / `reelcast_expression` | Current conversational target identities; product runtime/evidence separate | Produces or contributes to the Canonical Interview Source Package and Asset Package Spec | Interview Expression product → Pipeline derivative jobs | First-class source admission path after product gates |
| imported interview source | New first-class source admission | No Brief history may be invented; retrospective tags remain labeled until confirmed | Import/transcribe/align → Canonical Interview Source Package | Included in Release 1 eligibility |


# Success Metrics and Counter-Metrics

## Release 1 success metrics

- One real Activative or imported interview is admitted into a complete, rights-aware Canonical Interview Source Package.
- One source-led talking-head short uses original A-roll, exact source spans, word-safe EDL, real rendering, rendered-boundary evaluation, and bounded repair.
- One source-grounded Carousel or SuperVisual is produced from the same package with exact slide/frame lineage.
- At least one meaningful operator correction becomes a complete HumanResolutionEpisode and selective rerun.
- Every accepted derivative resolves to the exact Harness, binding, source package, source spans, JIT Capsule, typed program, runtime, evaluator, and execution fingerprint.
- Zero ineligible retrieval objects enter JIT context; hard negatives include wrong-category, superseded, restricted, and unsupported candidates.
- No synthetic URI, dry-run marker, or model self-report counts as a real artifact.
- Format 02 remains absent from active bindings, Studio surfaces, benchmarks, and release claims.
- Cancellation, replay, and source/version invalidation preserve history and reuse unaffected checkpoints.
- Rights, consent, quote/voice provenance, and publication authority pass before ship.

## Product metrics after expansion

- Operator review minutes and interventions per accepted derivative and per batch.
- Source-package admission accuracy, alignment correction rate, and time to approved Asset Package Spec.
- Expression Moment precision, recall, contextual-truth failure, and operator acceptance.
- Source-span reuse, duplicate-output rate, cross-derivative contradiction, and selective invalidation efficiency.
- A-roll coverage, cut-boundary failure, caption/audio correctness, and whole-short semantic acceptance.
- Retrieval top-K coverage, invalid-eligibility rate, contradiction coverage, and downstream decision lift.
- Programmed Model precision, argument accuracy, over-edit rate, escalation quality, latency, cost, and variance.
- HumanResolutionEpisode completeness, attribution quality, retrieval usefulness, and later shadow improvement.
- Real artifact, recovery, fallback, and publication success by runtime and profile.

## Counter-metrics

- Higher output volume with weaker source truth or more editorial overstatement.
- Lower cost achieved through silent model, provider, or runtime substitution.
- Fewer human gates caused by hidden automation rather than better precision.
- A short that looks polished but removes the speaker's meaningful reaction or changes context.
- Static derivatives that appear source-backed but use invented quotes or unsupported claims.
- Immediate training volume that violates rights, scope, or test isolation.


# Non-Goals and Anti-Goals

- Rewriting the Atomic Harness Builder or introducing a second semantic Harness.
- Treating the Pipeline as the Interview Expression product, Visual Asset Editor, Delegation Protocol, or Studio state authority.
- Building one universal creative agent, one universal editor model, or one universal aesthetic score.
- Treating every uploaded video as if it came from an Activative Interview Brief.
- Treating planned tags as actual expression or model inference as operator confirmation.
- Replacing the talking-head source with a generated script and still labeling the result a source-led interview short.
- Presenting paraphrases, condensations, synthetic voice, or editorial bridges as verbatim source expression.
- Allowing a timeline UI, React component, browser canvas, renderer workspace, or provider response to become canonical state.
- Copying external projects without bounded capability extraction and license/security review.
- Making OpenMontage, video-use, Remotion, HyperFrames, OpenVideo, lineCode, OmniShotCut, CutClaw, Stretchy, OKF, GNM, or an embedding model product authority.
- Using GNM demographic sampling as identity truth for a real participant or semantic expression labels as emotional truth.
- Activating Format 02 from predecessor code, registries, or demos.
- Updating production weights, Skills, recipes, or doctrine directly from live clicks.
- Equating local implementation completion, real bounded output, production readiness, evaluator certification, and product certification.


# MVP and Release Plan

## Release 0 — Authority, source, and PRD reconciliation

- Ratify this PRD V1.1 and decisions D041–D054.
- Verify operator-local terminal state and reconcile it into Program Control.
- Freeze and hash the predecessor archive and source crosswalk.
- Publish product-boundary amendments for Interview Expression, Pipeline, VAE/GNM, Delegation, and Studio.
- Validate all FR/Story/Tech-Spec ownership and issue bounded planning authority.

## Release 1 — Real source-first interview-to-batch proof

One real Activative Interview or imported interview:

- becomes a complete Canonical Interview Source Package;
- produces an approved Expression Ingredient Inventory / Asset Package Spec;
- launches a content batch;
- renders one source-led talking-head short with original A-roll;
- renders one source-grounded Carousel or SuperVisual from the same source;
- uses real files and exact source lineage;
- runs deterministic and independent evaluation;
- performs one bounded repair or human correction;
- records a HumanResolutionEpisode;
- exports a replayable audit bundle.

No Format 02 output is included.

## Release 1.1 — Retrieval, Revision Compiler, and static-profile evidence

- Benchmark CMF-OKF plus eligibility, lexical, dense, graph, visual/composition, and VLM reranking.
- Operate the Revision Compiler in shadow and review modes.
- Ratify bounded Carousel and SuperVisual profiles.
- Build rights-aware preference and repair corpora from real episodes.

## Release 2 — Edited-video archetype expansion

- Add more source-led short-video Harnesses and archetype routes.
- Add robust multi-take selection, long-video chunking/overlap, shot analysis, support-layer planning, and runtime fallback.
- Expand Remotion/HyperFrames motion blocks and operator timeline/canvas projections.

## Release 3 — VAE visual-production integration

- Execute authorized SAM3, matting, layered-generation, ComfyUI, and bounded GNM reference routes through VAE.
- Prove real demand/result/acknowledgement, geometry, evaluation, recovery, and source/identity lineage.

## Future — Format 02

Only after the current Builder emits and independent validation accepts the complete current Format 02 Harness may Program Control regenerate active runtime and Studio specifications.


# Risks and Mitigations

| Risk | Consequence | Mitigation |
|---|---|---|
| Source intention is confused with actual expression | The system routes content from a planned tag that the participant never expressed. | Distinct tag provenance states, exact source evidence, Analyst approval, and exclusion tests. |
| Imported interviews are treated as second-class or fabricated Brief sessions | Existing valuable footage cannot enter the full system, or false planning history is created. | Dual admission parity with explicit absent fields and retrospective inference labels. |
| A-roll is replaced by generated content | The short no longer embodies the original human expression. | Mandatory A-roll coverage and source-audio lineage for source-led short Harnesses. |
| Timeline UI becomes canonical state | Edits disappear on reload or bypass validation. | Adopt VideoEditProgram; UI emits typed commands and reconstructs from canonical records. |
| External code imports product authority or license obligations | The architecture drifts or creates distribution constraints. | Bounded capability extraction, source disposition, license/security review, adapter isolation. |
| GNM is used as identity/emotion truth | A real person's representation is fabricated or stereotyped. | VAE-only geometry role, approved source fitting/references, demographic-sampler prohibition, independent evaluation. |
| Human clicks become unscoped doctrine | One preference changes all future outputs. | HumanResolutionEpisode with narrow default scope; offline evidence and promotion gates. |
| Retrieval returns similar but ineligible knowledge | A wrong-category or superseded recipe guides production. | Deterministic eligibility first, contradiction/exclusion evidence, retrieval receipts. |
| Batch changes trigger total regeneration | Cost and latency rise and accepted work is lost. | Dependency graph, immutable versions, selective invalidation, checkpoint reuse. |
| Format 02 is prematurely revived | Historical prototypes are represented as current product capability. | Mechanical deferral checks and absence of active routes, specs, model claims, or release evidence. |

# Assumptions and Open Questions

## Assumptions

- The current Builder can represent or be amended to represent accepted source-package types, derivative job requirements, Skills/recipes, Programmed Model claims, runtime capabilities, and evaluation obligations without becoming the runtime.
- Interview Expression can own both Brief-led and imported-source admission and can emit the source and Asset Package objects defined here.
- The predecessor CMF Studio source remains available as migration evidence and can be separated from obsolete authority and fake-result behavior.
- One real source-led short and one static derivative can be produced with available rights and operator review.
- Program Control will establish the Atomic Harness Pipeline as a fourth independent product authority after reconciliation.

## Open questions requiring Tech Spec or human decision

1. Which exact current Interview Expression repository and contracts become canonical for the two admission paths?
2. Which transcription/diarization stack is the first reference implementation, and what human correction thresholds apply?
3. Which predecessor VideoEditProgram contracts become canonical after field-by-field migration?
4. Which timeline UI foundation passes license, integer-frame, accessibility, performance, and command-round-trip tests?
5. Does Remotion serve as master compositor for Release 1, with HyperFrames as bounded motion slots, or does a specific job use HyperFrames as master?
6. Which source rights and consent templates permit operational retrieval, publication, and later model training?
7. Which Carousel or SuperVisual profile becomes the first static derivative?
8. Which independent evaluator and human calibration set qualify the source-led short and static derivative?
9. Which Programmed Model claim is first: Moment retrieval, A-roll EDL, static operation compilation, or Revision Compiler?
10. Which Supabase or other durable control-plane services are approved, and which long-running jobs remain external workers?
11. Which VAE release and Delegation package are current after Program Control reconciliation?
12. What exact evidence later reopens Format 02 planning?


# Implementation Readiness Handoff

## Required gates

- `SR-GATE-001`: verify operator-local receipts and publish one reconciled current product status.
- `AUTH-GATE-001`: ratify the Pipeline and cross-product source-first amendments.
- `PRD-GATE-001`: ratify 27 features, 162 FRs, 85 NFRs, and decisions D041–D054.
- `SOURCE-GATE-001`: approve exact predecessor reuse and external license/security dispositions.
- `INTERVIEW-GATE-001`: approve Canonical Interview Source Package and dual-admission ownership.
- `CONTRACT-GATE-001`: publish source, batch, node, program, revision, episode, receipt, and runtime contracts.
- `RIGHTS-GATE-001`: approve participant/source rights and model-training eligibility policies.
- `F02-GATE-001`: confirm Format 02 remains deferred and absent from active implementation.
- `PLANNING-GATE-001`: validate one primary Story and candidate Tech Spec owner for every FR.
- `CAPSULE-GATE-001`: issue bounded Development Capsules and exact file allowlists before coding.

## Implementation posture

The mode remains brownfield activation and rebinding. The Builder is not redesigned. The predecessor monolith is not restarted. Exact runtime, UI, contract, and test assets are extracted behind current product boundaries. Planning artifacts are not implementation authority.

## Proposed target

`target://04_ATOMIC_HARNESS_PIPELINE/`, plus bounded amendments to Interview Expression, Visual Asset Editor, Delegation Protocol, Program Control, and the shared Conscious Activations Studio.

## Next artifacts after ratification

1. Final product ownership amendment and authority receipt.
2. Canonical source, batch, program, revision, episode, and retrieval schemas.
3. CBAR-hardened Epics and vertical Stories.
4. Candidate Tech Specs converted into accepted implementation specs.
5. Exact source/path allowlists and Development Capsules.
6. Source-first Release 1 evidence campaign.


# Programmed Model Recommendations

This table defines benchmark hypotheses, not selected models or training authority. The product unit is the complete Model Program and harness, not weights alone.

| ID | Program family | Bounded claim | Owner/scope | Candidate model posture | Critical limit |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| PM-SRC-01 | Source tag and evidence classifier | Classify proposed tags as planned, observed, inferred, confirmed, rejected, or unsupported using source references | Interview Expression | Small text model after labeled tag data | Never creates authority or source evidence |
| PM-SRC-02 | Expression Moment Hunter | Retrieve and propose source-backed spans with context, audio events, keyframes, and archetype opportunities | Interview Expression | 1–4B text/multimodal candidate; stronger teacher | Cannot approve, route, or invent quotes |
| PM-BATCH-01 | Archetype and Harness router | Rank eligible derivative routes after deterministic filters | Pipeline | 1B structured model or retrieval/reranker | No route outside current Harness/profile authority |
| PM-RET-01 | Semantic ranker | Rank eligible Skills, recipes, precedents, code, and source moments | All | Nemotron-3-Embed-1B candidate; 8B quality anchor | Text/code ranking only; eligibility and visual relevance remain separate |
| PM-VID-01 | A-roll EDL compiler | Compile approved source spans into word-safe EDL and output-time map | Short video | 1–4B structured model | Source meaning and cut correctness are hard gates |
| PM-VID-02 | Visual shot/take selector | Compare candidate source spans and frames for archetype function and expression continuity | Short video | 4B multimodal candidate; 27B teacher | Must retain transcript/source context |
| PM-VID-03 | Support-layer planner | Select evidence, B-roll, caption, keyframe, and motion-block functions around A-roll | Short video | 4B multimodal candidate | No decorative unsupported inserts |
| PM-REV-01 | Revision Compiler | Translate operator language into the smallest valid typed change program | Studio/Pipeline | 1–4B model with category-specific claims | Deterministic authority/minimality validation; escalation on ambiguity |
| PM-STA-01 | Static strategy and operation compiler | Retrieve a valid recipe and compile BBOX/text/annotation operations | Carousel/SuperVisual | 4B multimodal strategy plus 1B structured executor | PRETEXT/geometry and independent evaluation gate output |
| PM-ANI-01 | Animation derivative planner | Compile source-grounded scenes, audio/quote bindings, keyframes, and rig/motion requirements | Non-Format-02 animation | 4B planner plus structured executor | Does not activate or impersonate Format 02 |
| PM-EVAL-01 | Independent visual/temporal evaluator | Assess judgment dimensions after deterministic checks | Category-specific | Independent multimodal model with human calibration | Producer cannot approve itself |
| PM-COMP-01 | Atomic tool router | Select one obvious operation in mature bounded tool subsets | Mature subsets | Needle-class late compression experiment | Only after stable stronger baseline and deterministic validation |
| PM-GNM-01 | Future bounded GNM control translator | Translate approved geometric expression/pose requirements into named GNM controls | VAE only | Small structured model after deterministic baseline | No identity/emotion inference; source-backed references required |

# Exact Source Reference Convention

Every `SRC-*` identifier resolves through the original source crosswalk plus `governance/SOURCE_REGISTER_ADDITIONS.csv`. Local files use SHA-256. Repository references use the observed blob SHA when available. External evidence never determines authority.
